/root/fideslib/src/CKKS/Ciphertext.cuh

     1	//
     2	// Created by carlosad on 24/04/24.
     3	//
     4	
     5	#ifndef FIDESLIB_CKKS_CIPHERTEXT_CUH
     6	#define FIDESLIB_CKKS_CIPHERTEXT_CUH
     7	
     8	#include <source_location>
     9	#include "RNSPoly.cuh"
    10	#include "forwardDefs.cuh"
    11	#include "openfhe-interface/RawCiphertext.cuh"
    12	
    13	namespace FIDESlib::CKKS {
    14	
    15	/**
    16	 * @brief Global flag controlling whether hoisted rotation optimisation is enabled.
    17	 *
    18	 * This can be toggled at runtime to switch between the standard hoisted-rotation
    19	 * implementation and the fused hoisted‑rotation variant.
    20	 */
    21	extern bool hoistRotateFused;
    22	
    23	/**
    24	 * @class Ciphertext
    25	 * @brief Represents a ciphertext in the CKKS scheme.
    26	 *
    27	 * The ciphertext holds two RNSPoly components (c0 and c1) together with
    28	 * associated metadata (key identifier, noise level, scaling factor, etc.).
    29	 * It provides arithmetic operations, key‑switching, rotations and
    30	 * rescaling.  Most operations maintain the level information and may
    31	 * automatically perform rescaling or modulus‑down conversion as required
    32	 * by the CKKS protocol.
    33	 */
    34	class Ciphertext {
    35	    /** @brief Identifier string for NVTX profiling. */
    36	    static constexpr const char* loc{"Ciphertext"};
    37	    /** @brief NVTX range object for profiling this class' methods. */
    38	    CudaNvtxRange my_range;
    39	
    40	   public:
    41	    /** @brief Identifier for the key associated with this ciphertext. */
    42	    KeyHash keyID{""};
    43	    /** @brief Reference to the CKKS context owning this ciphertext. */
    44	    Context& cc_;
    45	    /** @brief Reference to the context data (metadata) for this ciphertext. */
    46	    ContextData& cc;
    47	    /** @brief The two polynomial components of the ciphertext (c0 and c1). */
    48	    RNSPoly c0, c1;
    49	    /** @brief Accumulated noise factor for this ciphertext. */
    50	    double NoiseFactor = 0;
    51	    /** @brief Discrete noise level indicator. */
    52	    int NoiseLevel = {1};
    53	    /** @brief Number of slots (vector length) encoded in the ciphertext. */
    54	    int slots = 0;
    55	
    56	    /**
    57	     * @brief Move constructor. Transfers ownership of the internal resources
    58	     *        from another Ciphertext instance.
    59	     *
    60	     * @param ct_moved Rvalue reference to the source Ciphertext.
    61	     */
    62	    Ciphertext(Ciphertext&& ct_moved) noexcept;
    63	
    64	    /**
    65	     * @brief Constructs an empty Ciphertext bound to a given context.
    66	     *
    67	     * The created ciphertext has uninitialised polynomial components and zero noise.
    68	     *
    69	     * @param cc Reference to the CKKS Context the ciphertext belongs to.
    70	     */
    71	    explicit Ciphertext(Context& cc);
    72	
    73	    /**
    74	     * @brief Constructs a Ciphertext from a serialized RawCipherText.
    75	     *
    76	     * This loads polynomial data and metadata from the raw representation.
    77	     *
    78	     * @param cc   Reference to the CKKS Context.
    79	     * @param rawct Serialized representation of a ciphertext.
    80	     */
    81	    Ciphertext(Context& cc, const RawCipherText& rawct);
    82	
    83	    /** @brief Destructor. Releases any allocated resources. */
    84	    ~Ciphertext();
    85	
    86	    /**
    87	     * @brief Copies only the metadata fields from another ciphertext.
    88	     *
    89	     * This does **not** copy polynomial data.
    90	     *
    91	     * @param a Source ciphertext to copy metadata from.
    92	     */
    93	    void copyMetadata(const Ciphertext& a);
    94	
    95	    /**
    96	     * @brief Merges metadata from two ciphertexts into *this*.
    97	     *
    98	     * Used after operations that combine two ciphertexts.
    99	     *
   100	     * @param a First operand.
   101	     * @param b Second operand.
   102	     */
   103	    void addMetadata(const Ciphertext& a, const Ciphertext& b);
   104	
   105	    /**
   106	     * @brief Merges metadata from a ciphertext and a plaintext into *this*.
   107	     *
   108	     * @param a Ciphertext operand.
   109	     * @param b Plaintext operand.
   110	     */
   111	    void addMetadata(const Ciphertext& a, const Plaintext& b);
   112	
   113	    /**
   114	     * @brief Merges metadata appropriate for multiplication of two ciphertexts.
   115	     *
   116	     * @param a First operand.
   117	     * @param b Second operand.
   118	     */
   119	    void multMetadata(const Ciphertext& a, const Ciphertext& b);
   120	
   121	    /**
   122	     * @brief Merges metadata for multiplication of a ciphertext with a plaintext.
   123	     *
   124	     * @param a Ciphertext operand.
   125	     * @param b Plaintext operand.
   126	     */
   127	    void multMetadata(const Ciphertext& a, const Plaintext& b);
   128	
   129	    /**
   130	     * @brief Normalises a rotation index to the valid range for the current slot count.
   131	     *
   132	     * The function makes the index positive, maps it into `[0, slots)` and, if the
   133	     * index exceeds half the slot count, adds `N/2 - slots` to map it into the
   134	     * underlying NTT domain.
   135	     *
   136	     * @param index Desired rotation index (may be negative).
   137	     * @return Normalized index within `[0, slots)`.
   138	     */
   139	    int normalyzeIndex(int index) const;
   140	
   141	    /**
   142	     * @brief Loads ciphertext data from a RawCipherText representation.
   143	     *
   144	     * @param rawct Serialized ciphertext to load.
   145	     */
   146	    void load(const RawCipherText& rawct);
   147	
   148	    /**
   149	     * @brief Stores the current ciphertext into a RawCipherText representation.
   150	     *
   151	     * @param rawct Destination object that will receive the serialized data.
   152	     */
   153	    void store(RawCipherText& rawct);
   154	
   155	    /**
   156	     * @brief Adds another ciphertext to *this* (in‑place).
   157	     *
   158	     * The method ensures both ciphertexts are on the same level, performing
   159	     * rescaling or level adjustments when required by the current
   160	     * `rescaleTechnique`.  It may invoke `adjustForAddOrSub` and, if that
   161	     * fails, create a temporary copy of `b` with aligned scaling before
   162	     * retrying.  After the polynomial addition, metadata is merged via
   163	     * `addMetadata`.  The operation count for `ADD` is incremented.
   164	     *
   165	     * @param b Ciphertext to add.
   166	     */
   167	    void add(const Ciphertext& b);
   168	
   169	    /**
   170	     * @brief Subtracts another ciphertext from *this* (in‑place).
   171	     *
   172	     * Mirrors the behaviour of `add` but uses subtraction on the polynomial
   173	     * components.  Rescaling, level alignment and metadata handling follow the
   174	     * same logic as in `add`.
   175	     *
   176	     * @param b Ciphertext to subtract.
   177	     */
   178	    void sub(const Ciphertext& b);
   179	
   180	    /**
   181	     * @brief Adds a plaintext to *this* ciphertext (in‑place).
   182	     *
   183	     * Handles automatic rescaling when the plaintext and ciphertext have
   184	     * mismatched levels or noise.  For flexible rescaling techniques it may
   185	     * create a temporary adjusted plaintext before performing the addition.
   186	     * After the operation, metadata is merged via `addMetadata`.
   187	     *
   188	     * @param b Plaintext operand.
   189	     */
   190	    void addPt(const Plaintext& b);
   191	
   192	    /**
   193	     * @brief Subtracts a plaintext from *this* ciphertext (in‑place).
   194	     *
   195	     * The semantics are analogous to `addPt` but perform subtraction on `c0`.
   196	     *
   197	     * @param pt Plaintext operand.
   198	     */
   199	    void subPt(const Plaintext& pt);
   200	
   201	    /**
   202	     * @brief Adds a scalar (double) to both polynomial components.
   203	     *
   204	     * The scalar is first converted to the appropriate modulus representation
   205	     * via `ElemForEvalAddOrSub`.  The sign of the scalar is handled by
   206	     * converting the element to its complement when `c < 0`.  No metadata
   207	     * updates are performed.
   208	     *
   209	     * @param c Scalar value to add.
   210	     */
   211	    void addScalar(const double c);
   212	
   213	    /**
   214	     * @brief Multiplies *this* ciphertext by a plaintext.
   215	     *
   216	     * If the current rescaling technique requires matching noise levels,
   217	     * the method may rescale the ciphertext or adjust the plaintext
   218	     * (creating a temporary copy) before multiplication.  After the
   219	     * component‑wise multiplication, metadata is merged via `multMetadata`.
   220	     * If `rescale` is true and the technique is `FIXEDMANUAL`, the
   221	     * ciphertext is rescaled and the noise factor/level are updated.
   222	     *
   223	     * @param b Plaintext operand.
   224	     * @param rescale If true, performs rescaling after multiplication.
   225	     */
   226	    void multPt(const Plaintext& b, bool rescale = false);
   227	
   228	    /**
   229	     * @brief Multiplies a ciphertext `c` by a plaintext and stores the result in *this*.
   230	     *
   231	     * Equivalent to copying `c` into *this* and then invoking `multPt(b, rescale)`.
   232	     *
   233	     * @param c Ciphertext operand.
   234	     * @param b Plaintext operand.
   235	     * @param rescale Perform rescaling after multiplication if true.
   236	     */
   237	    void multPt(const Ciphertext& c, const Plaintext& b, bool rescale = false);
   238	
   239	    /**
   240	     * @brief Computes `*this + (c * b)` in a single fused operation.
   241	     *
   242	     * The method adds ciphertext `c * b` to *this* and optionally rescales.  
   243	     * Metadata is merged via `multMetadata`.
   244	     *
   245	     * @param c Ciphertext to add.
   246	     * @param b Plaintext to multiply.
   247	     * @param rescale Perform rescaling after multiplication if true.
   248	     */
   249	    void addMultPt(const Ciphertext& c, const Plaintext& b, bool rescale = false);
   250	
   251	    /**
   252	     * @brief Multiplies *this* by another ciphertext.
   253	     *
   254	     * Handles level alignment and possible rescaling according to the current
   255	     * `rescaleTechnique`.  If necessary, the method calls `adjustForMult`
   256	     * (creating a temporary copy of `b` when alignment fails).  The actual
   257	     * multiplication is performed before a key‑switch operation.  Metadata is
   258	     * merged via `multMetadata`.  The operation count for `MULT` is incremented.
   259	     *
   260	     * @param b Ciphertext multiplier.
   261	     * @param rescale Perform rescaling after multiplication if true.
   262	     * @param moddown Perform modulus down‑conversion if true.
   263	     */
   264	    void mult(const Ciphertext& b, bool rescale = false, bool moddown = true);
   265	
   266	    /**
   267	     * @brief Multiplies two ciphertexts and stores the result in *this*.
   268	     *
   269	     * This overload forwards to the two‑argument version, using `b` and `c`
   270	     * as the two multiplicands.  It exists for convenience when the two
   271	     * operands are already separate objects.
   272	     *
   273	     * @param b First operand.
   274	     * @param c Second operand.
   275	     * @param rescale Perform rescaling after multiplication if true.
   276	     */
   277	    void mult(const Ciphertext& b, const Ciphertext& c, bool rescale = false);
   278	
   279	    /**
   280	     * @brief Multiplies both polynomial components by a scalar without pre‑checks.
   281	     *
   282	     * The scalar is converted to the appropriate modulus element via
   283	     * `ElemForEvalMult`.  If `rescale` is true and the technique is
   284	     * `FIXEDMANUAL`, the ciphertext is rescaled after multiplication.
   285	     *
   286	     * @param c Scalar multiplier.
   287	     * @param rescale Perform rescaling after multiplication if true.
   288	     */
   289	    void multScalarNoPrecheck(const double c, bool rescale = false);
   290	
   291	    /**
   292	     * @brief Multiplies both polynomial components by a scalar, performing necessary checks.
   293	     *
   294	     * For flexible rescaling techniques the method may rescale the ciphertext
   295	     * when the noise level is 2.  The scalar is converted using
   296	     * `ElemForEvalMult` and the multiplication is applied to both components.
   297	     * Metadata (noise level/factor) is updated accordingly; if `rescale`
   298	     * is true and the technique is `FIXEDMANUAL`, a rescaling step follows.
   299	     *
   300	     * @param c Scalar multiplier.
   301	     * @param rescale Perform rescaling after multiplication if true.
   302	     */
   303	    void multScalar(const double c, bool rescale = false);
   304	
   305	    /**
   306	     * @brief Multiplies a ciphertext `b` by a scalar and stores the result in *this*.
   307	     *
   308	     * The method copies `b` into *this* and then calls `multScalar(c,
   309	     * rescale)`.  It is useful when the caller wishes to keep `b` unchanged.
   310	     *
   311	     * @param b Ciphertext operand.
   312	     * @param c Scalar multiplier.
   313	     * @param rescale Perform rescaling after multiplication if true.
   314	     */
   315	    void multScalar(const Ciphertext& b, const double c, bool rescale = false);
   316	
   317	    /**
   318	     * @brief Squares the ciphertext (i.e., multiplies it by itself).
   319	     *
   320	     * After the multiplication the metadata (noise level/factor) is updated.
   321	     * If `rescale` is true and the technique is `FIXEDMANUAL`, a rescaling
   322	     * step follows.
   323	     *
   324	     * @param rescale Perform rescaling after squaring if true.
   325	     */
   326	    void square(bool rescale = false);
   327	
   328	    /**
   329	     * @brief Squares the source ciphertext `src` and stores the result in *this*.
   330	     *
   331	     * Equivalent to copying `src` into *this* and then calling `square(rescale)`.
   332	     *
   333	     * @param src Source ciphertext to square.
   334	     * @param rescale Perform rescaling after squaring if true.
   335	     */
   336	    void square(const Ciphertext& src, bool rescale = false);
   337	
   338	    /**
   339	     * @brief Rotates the slots of the ciphertext by `index` positions.
   340	     *
   341	     * The index is normalised using `normalyzeIndex`.  Depending on the
   342	     * `moddown` flag, a modulus‑down conversion may be performed after the
   343	     * rotation.
   344	     *
   345	     * @param index Number of slots to rotate (positive = left).
   346	     * @param moddown Perform modulus down‑conversion after rotation if true.
   347	     */
   348	    void rotate(const int index, bool moddown = true);
   349	
   350	    /**
   351	     * @brief Rotates ciphertext `c` by `index` slots and stores the result in *this*.
   352	     *
   353	     * This overload copies `c` into *this* and then calls the single‑argument
   354	     * `rotate(index, true)`.
   355	     *
   356	     * @param c Source ciphertext.
   357	     * @param index Number of slots to rotate.
   358	     */
   359	    void rotate(const Ciphertext& c, const int index);
   360	
   361	    /**
   362	     * @brief Computes the complex conjugate of ciphertext `c` and stores it in *this*.
   363	     *
   364	     * The operation is performed component‑wise and updates the operation
   365	     * count for `CONJUGATE`.
   366	     *
   367	     * @param c Source ciphertext.
   368	     */
   369	    void conjugate(const Ciphertext& c);
   370	
   371	    /**
   372	     * @brief Performs modulus down‑conversion on the ciphertext.
   373	     *
   374	     * Both polynomial components are down‑converted; when `free` is true the
   375	     * temporary special limbs are released.
   376	     *
   377	     * @param free If true, frees intermediate buffers after conversion.
   378	     */
   379	    void modDown(bool free = false);
   380	
   381	    /** @brief Increases the modulus level of the ciphertext (level up). */
   382	    void modUp();
   383	
   384	    /** @brief Rescales the ciphertext to the next level, adjusting scaling factor. */
   385	    void rescale();
   386	
   387	    /**
   388	     * @brief Grows the ciphertext to at least `level` by performing necessary modulus upgrades.
   389	     *
   390	     * The method ensures both components reach the requested level, generating
   391	     * special limbs if required.
   392	     *
   393	     * @param level Desired minimum level.
   394	     */
   395	    void growToLevel(int level);
   396	
   397	    /** @brief Drops the ciphertext to a lower level, discarding higher moduli. 
   398	    
   399	        @todo adjust the scale on FLEXIBLE modes
   400	    */
   401	    void dropToLevel(int level);
   402	
   403	    /**
   404	     * @brief Returns the current modulus level of the ciphertext.
   405	     *
   406	     * @return Current level index (both components share the same level).
   407	     */
   408	    [[nodiscard]] int getLevel() const;
   409	
   410	    /**
   411	     * @brief Performs an automorphism on the ciphertext.
   412	     *
   413	     * The automorphism is applied to both polynomial components; the `br`
   414	     * argument is passed to the underlying `RNSPoly::automorph` method and
   415	     * is implementation‑specific.
   416	     *
   417	     * @param index Automorphism index.
   418	     * @param br    Additional parameter used by the underlying implementation.
   419	     */
   420	    void automorph(const int index, const int br);

    68	: my_range(std::move(ct_moved.my_range)), keyID(std::move(ct_moved.keyID)), cc_(ct_moved.cc_), cc(*cc_), c0(std::move(ct_moved.c0)), c1(std::move(ct_moved.c1)),

    72	Ciphertext::Ciphertext(Context& cc)
    73	: my_range(loc, LIFETIME), cc_((assert(cc != nullptr), CudaNvtxStart(std::string{ sc::current().function_name() }.substr()), cc)), cc(*cc_),
    74	  c0(cc->getAuxilarPoly()), c1(cc->getAuxilarPoly()) {
    75		c0.dropToLevel(-1);
    76		c1.dropToLevel(-1);
    77		c0.SetModUp(false);
    78		c1.SetModUp(false);
    79		CudaNvtxStop();
    80	}

    86	Ciphertext::~Ciphertext() {
    87		if (!c1.GPU.empty())
    88			cc.returnAuxilarPoly(std::move(c1));
    89		if (!c0.GPU.empty())
    90			cc.returnAuxilarPoly(std::move(c0));
    91	}

    93	void Ciphertext::copyMetadata(const Ciphertext& a) {
    94		assert(this->getLevel() == a.getLevel());
    95		this->slots		  = a.slots;
    96		this->keyID		  = a.keyID;
    97		this->NoiseLevel  = a.NoiseLevel;
    98		this->NoiseFactor = a.NoiseFactor;
    99	}
   100	
   101	void Ciphertext::addMetadata(const Ciphertext& a, const Ciphertext& b) {
   102		assert(this->getLevel() == a.getLevel());
   103		if (RESCALE_TECHNIQUE::FLEXIBLEAUTO == cc.rescaleTechnique || RESCALE_TECHNIQUE::FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT == cc.rescaleTechnique) {
   104			assert(a.getLevel() == b.getLevel());
   105			// assert(abs(a.NoiseFactor - b.NoiseFactor) < a.NoiseFactor / 1e9);
   106		}
   107		this->slots = std::max(a.slots, b.slots);
   108		assert(a.keyID == b.keyID);
   109		this->keyID = a.keyID;
   110		assert(a.NoiseLevel == b.NoiseLevel);
   111		this->NoiseLevel = a.NoiseLevel;
   112	
   113		this->NoiseFactor = a.NoiseFactor;
   114	}
   115	
   116	void Ciphertext::addMetadata(const Ciphertext& a, const Plaintext& b) {
   117		assert(this->getLevel() == a.getLevel());
   118		if (RESCALE_TECHNIQUE::FLEXIBLEAUTO == cc.rescaleTechnique || RESCALE_TECHNIQUE::FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT == cc.rescaleTechnique) {
   119			assert(a.getLevel() == b.c0.getLevel());
   120			// assert(a.NoiseFactor == b.NoiseFactor);
   121		}
   122		this->slots = std::max(a.slots, b.slots);
   123		this->keyID = a.keyID;
   124		assert(a.NoiseLevel == b.NoiseLevel);
   125		this->NoiseLevel  = a.NoiseLevel;
   126		this->NoiseFactor = a.NoiseFactor;
   127	}

   129	void Ciphertext::multMetadata(const Ciphertext& a, const Ciphertext& b) {
   130		assert(this->getLevel() == a.getLevel());
   131		if (RESCALE_TECHNIQUE::FLEXIBLEAUTO == cc.rescaleTechnique || RESCALE_TECHNIQUE::FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT == cc.rescaleTechnique) {
   132			assert(a.getLevel() == b.getLevel());
   133			// assert(a.NoiseFactor == b.NoiseFactor);
   134		}
   135		this->slots = std::max(a.slots, b.slots);
   136		assert(a.keyID == b.keyID);
   137		this->keyID = a.keyID;
   138		assert(a.NoiseLevel == b.NoiseLevel);
   139		this->NoiseLevel  = a.NoiseLevel + b.NoiseLevel;
   140		this->NoiseFactor = a.NoiseFactor * b.NoiseFactor;
   141	}
   142	
   143	void Ciphertext::multMetadata(const Ciphertext& a, const Plaintext& b) {
   144		assert(this->getLevel() == a.getLevel());
   145		if (RESCALE_TECHNIQUE::FLEXIBLEAUTO == cc.rescaleTechnique || RESCALE_TECHNIQUE::FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT == cc.rescaleTechnique) {
   146			assert(a.getLevel() == b.c0.getLevel());
   147			// assert(a.NoiseFactor == b.NoiseFactor);
   148		}
   149		this->slots = std::max(a.slots, b.slots);
   150		this->keyID = a.keyID;
   151		assert(a.NoiseLevel == b.NoiseLevel);
   152		this->NoiseLevel = a.NoiseLevel + b.NoiseLevel;
   153	
   154		this->NoiseFactor = a.NoiseFactor * b.NoiseFactor;
   155	}
   156	
   157	int Ciphertext::normalyzeIndex(int index) const {
   158		index = index % slots;
   159		if (index < 0)
   160			index += slots;
   161		if (index > slots / 2)
   162			index += cc.N / 2 - slots;
   163		return index;
   164	}
   165	
   166	void Ciphertext::add(const Ciphertext& b) {
   167		CudaNvtxRange r(std::string{ sc::current().function_name() }.substr());
   168		CKKS::SetCurrentContext(cc_);
   169		assert(keyID == b.keyID);
   170		if (cc.rescaleTechnique == FIXEDAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT) {
   171			if (!adjustForAddOrSub(b)) {
   172				Ciphertext b_(cc_);
   173				b_.copy(b);
   174				if (b_.adjustForAddOrSub(*this))
   175					add(b_);
   176				else
   177					assert(false);
   178				return;
   179			}
   180		}
   181	
   182		if (cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT) {
   183			assert(this->getLevel() == b.getLevel());
   184		} else if (getLevel() > b.getLevel()) {
   185			c0.dropToLevel(b.getLevel());
   186			c1.dropToLevel(b.getLevel());
   187		}
   188		op_count[OPS::ADD]++;
   189	
   190		c0.add(b.c0);
   191		c1.add(b.c1);
   192	
   193		this->addMetadata(*this, b);
   194	}
   195	
   196	void Ciphertext::sub(const Ciphertext& b) {
   197		CudaNvtxRange r(std::string{ sc::current().function_name() }.substr());
   198		CKKS::SetCurrentContext(cc_);
   199		assert(keyID == b.keyID);
   200		if (cc.rescaleTechnique == FIXEDAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT) {
   201			if (!adjustForAddOrSub(b)) {
   202				Ciphertext b_(cc_);
   203				b_.copy(b);
   204				if (b_.adjustForAddOrSub(*this))
   205					sub(b_);
   206				else
   207					assert(false);
   208				return;
   209			}
   210		}
   211	
   212		if (cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT) {
   213			assert(this->getLevel() == b.getLevel());
   214		} else if (getLevel() > b.getLevel()) {
   215			c0.dropToLevel(b.getLevel());
   216			c1.dropToLevel(b.getLevel());
   217		}
   218		op_count[OPS::ADD]++;
   219	
   220		c0.sub(b.c0);
   221		c1.sub(b.c1);
   222	
   223		this->addMetadata(*this, b);
   224	}
   225	
   226	void Ciphertext::addPt(const Plaintext& b) {
   227		CudaNvtxRange r(std::string{ sc::current().function_name() }.substr());
   228		CKKS::SetCurrentContext(cc_);
   229		if (cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT || cc.rescaleTechnique == FIXEDAUTO) {
   230			if (b.NoiseLevel == 1 && NoiseLevel == 2 && b.c0.getLevel() == getLevel() - 1) {
   231				this->rescale();
   232			}
   233	
   234			if (b.c0.getLevel() != this->getLevel()) {
   235				Plaintext b_(cc_);
   236				if (!b_.adjustPlaintextToCiphertext(b, *this)) {
   237					assert(false);
   238				} else {
   239					addPt(b_);
   240				}
   241				return;
   242			}
   243		}
   244		assert(NoiseLevel == b.NoiseLevel);
   245		op_count[OPS::ADDPT]++;
   246	
   247		c0.add(b.c0);
   248	
   249		this->addMetadata(*this, b);
   250	}
   251	
   252	void Ciphertext::subPt(const Plaintext& b) {
   253		CudaNvtxRange r(std::string{ sc::current().function_name() }.substr());
   254		CKKS::SetCurrentContext(cc_);
   255		if (cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT || cc.rescaleTechnique == FIXEDAUTO) {
   256			if (b.NoiseLevel == 1 && NoiseLevel == 2 && b.c0.getLevel() == getLevel() - 1) {
   257				this->rescale();
   258			}
   259	
   260			if (b.c0.getLevel() != this->getLevel()) {
   261				Plaintext b_(cc_);
   262				if (!b_.adjustPlaintextToCiphertext(b, *this)) {
   263					assert(false);
   264				} else {
   265					addPt(b_);
   266				}
   267				return;
   268			}
   269		}
   270		assert(NoiseLevel == b.NoiseLevel);
   271		op_count[OPS::ADDPT]++;
   272	
   273		c0.sub(b.c0);
   274	
   275		this->addMetadata(*this, b);
   276	}
   277	
   278	void Ciphertext::load(const RawCipherText& rawct) {
   279		CudaNvtxRange r(std::string{ sc::current().function_name() }.substr());
   280		CKKS::SetCurrentContext(cc_);
   281		keyID = rawct.keyid;
   282		c0.load(rawct.sub_0, rawct.moduli);
   283		c1.load(rawct.sub_1, rawct.moduli);
   284	
   285		NoiseLevel	= rawct.NoiseLevel;
   286		NoiseFactor = rawct.Noise;
   287		slots		= rawct.slots;
   288	}
   289	
   290	void Ciphertext::store(RawCipherText& rawct) {
   291		CudaNvtxRange r(std::string{ sc::current().function_name() }.substr());
   292	
   293		CKKS::SetCurrentContext(cc_);
   294		cudaDeviceSynchronize();
   295		rawct.numRes = c0.getLevel() + 1;
   296		rawct.sub_0.resize(rawct.numRes);
   297		rawct.sub_1.resize(rawct.numRes);
   298		c0.store(rawct.sub_0);
   299		c1.store(rawct.sub_1);
   300		rawct.N = cc.N;
   301		c0.sync();
   302		c1.sync();
   303	
   304		rawct.NoiseLevel = NoiseLevel;
   305		rawct.Noise		 = NoiseFactor;
   306		rawct.keyid		 = keyID;
   307		rawct.slots		 = slots; // TODO store other interesting metadata
   308		cudaDeviceSynchronize();
   309	}
   310	
   311	void Ciphertext::modDown(bool free) {
   312		CudaNvtxRange r(std::string{ sc::current().function_name() }.substr());
   313		CKKS::SetCurrentContext(cc_);
   314		c0.moddown(true, false, 0);
   315		c1.moddown(true, false, 1);
   316		if (free) {
   317			c0.freeSpecialLimbs();
   318			c1.freeSpecialLimbs();
   319		}
   320	}
   321	
   322	void Ciphertext::modUp() {
   323		CudaNvtxRange r(std::string{ sc::current().function_name() }.substr());
   324		CKKS::SetCurrentContext(cc_);
   325		// c0.modup();
   326		c1.modup();
   327	}
   328	
   329	void Ciphertext::multPt(const Plaintext& b, bool rescale) {
   330		CudaNvtxRange r(std::string{ sc::current().function_name() }.substr());
   331		CKKS::SetCurrentContext(cc_);
   332		constexpr bool PRINT = false;
   333		if (cc.rescaleTechnique == FIXEDAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT) {
   334			if constexpr (PRINT)
   335				std::cout << "multPt: Rescale input ciphertext" << std::endl;
   336			if (NoiseLevel == 2)
   337				this->rescale();
   338		}
   339	
   340		if (cc.rescaleTechnique == FIXEDAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT) {
   341			if (b.c0.getLevel() != this->getLevel() || b.NoiseLevel == 2 /*!hasSameScalingFactor(b)*/) {
   342				Plaintext b_(cc_);
   343				if constexpr (PRINT)
   344					std::cout << "multPt: adjust input plaintext" << std::endl;
   345	
   346				// if (!this->adju)
   347				if (!b_.adjustPlaintextToCiphertext(b, *this)) {
   348					if constexpr (PRINT)
   349						std::cout << "multPt: FAILED!" << std::endl;
   350					assert(false);
   351				} else {
   352					if (NoiseLevel == 2)
   353						this->rescale();
   354					if (b_.NoiseLevel == 2) {
   355						if constexpr (PRINT)
   356							std::cout << "multPt: Rescale input plaintext" << std::endl;
   357						b_.rescale();
   358					}
   359					multPt(b_, rescale);
   360				}
   361				return;
   362			}
   363		}
   364	
   365		assert(NoiseLevel < 2);
   366		assert(b.NoiseLevel < 2);
   367		op_count[OPS::MULTPT]++;
   368	
   369		c0.multPt(b.c0, rescale && cc.rescaleTechnique == CKKS::FIXEDMANUAL);
   370		c1.multPt(b.c0, rescale && cc.rescaleTechnique == CKKS::FIXEDMANUAL);
   371	
   372		this->multMetadata(*this, b);
   373		if (rescale && cc.rescaleTechnique == CKKS::FIXEDMANUAL) {
   374			NoiseFactor /= cc.param.ModReduceFactor.at(c0.getLevel() + 1);
   375			NoiseLevel -= 1;
   376		}
   377	}
   378	
   379	void Ciphertext::rescale() {
   380		CudaNvtxRange r(std::string{ sc::current().function_name() }.substr());
   381		CKKS::SetCurrentContext(cc_);
   382		// assert(this->NoiseLevel == 2);
   383		if (cc.rescaleTechnique != FIXEDMANUAL) {
   384			// this wouldn't do anything in OpenFHE
   385		}
   386		op_count[OPS::RESCALE]++;
   387	
   388		if constexpr (RESCALE_DOUBLE) {
   389			c0.rescaleDouble(c1);
   390		} else {
   391			c0.rescale();
   392			c1.rescale();
   393		}
   394	
   395		// Manage metadata
   396		NoiseFactor /= cc.param.ModReduceFactor.at(c0.getLevel() + 1);
   397		NoiseLevel -= 1;
   398	}
   399	
   400	/** "in" needs to have Digit and Gather limbs pre-generated */
   401	RNSPoly& MGPUkeySwitchCore(RNSPoly& in, const KeySwitchingKey& kskEval, const bool moddown) {
   402		{
   403			RNSPoly& aux = in.modup_ksk_moddown_mgpu(kskEval, moddown);
   404	
   405			return aux;
   406		}
   407	}
   408	
   409	void Ciphertext::mult(const Ciphertext& b, bool rescale, const bool moddown) {
   410		CudaNvtxRange r(std::string{ sc::current().function_name() }.substr());
   411		CKKS::SetCurrentContext(cc_);
   412		assert(keyID == b.keyID);
   413		if (cc.rescaleTechnique == FIXEDAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT) {
   414			if (!adjustForMult(b)) {
   415				Ciphertext b_(cc_);
   416				b_.copy(b);
   417				if (b_.adjustForMult(*this))
   418					mult(b_, rescale, moddown);
   419				else
   420					assert(false);

    99	    void setLevel(const int level);

    24	void RNSPoly::grow(int new_level, bool single_malloc, bool constant) {
    25	    if (level >= new_level)
    26	        return;
    27	    level = new_level;
    28	
    29	    // single_malloc = false;
    30	    //if (level == -1) {
    31	    //std::cout << "from 0" << std::endl;
    32	    if (!constant && (!single_malloc || (GPU.at(0).limb.size() > 0)) && GPU.at(0).bufferLIMB == nullptr) {
    33	        // TODO fix bug (check that limb size matches level)
    34	        int init = 0;
    35	        for (auto& g : GPU)
    36	            init += g.limb.size();
    37	
    38	        for (auto& g : GPU) {
    39	            g.generateLimbToLevel(new_level);
    40	        }
    41	        //for (int i = init; i <= new_level; ++i) {
    42	        //    GPU.at(cc.limbGPUid.at(i).x).generateLimb();
    43	        //}
    44	    } else {
    45	        //#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(GPU.size())
    46	        for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
    47	            //          OMP_ASSERT(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)GPU.size());
    48	            if (!constant) {
    49	                GPU.at(i).generateLimbSingleMalloc();
    50	            } else {
    51	                GPU.at(i).generateLimbConstant();
    52	            }
    53	        }
    54	    }
    55	}
    56	
    57	RNSPoly::RNSPoly(ContextData& context, int level, bool single_malloc, bool def_stream)
    58	    : uid(next_uid++), cc(context), level(-1) {
    59	
    60	    //#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(context.GPUid.size())
    61	    for (size_t i = 0u; i < context.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
    62	        cudaSetDevice(context.GPUid.at(i));
    63	        GPU.emplace_back(context, uid, &this->level, i, def_stream);
    64	    }
    65	    assert(level >= -1 && level <= cc.L);
    66	    grow(level, single_malloc);
    67	}
    68	
    69	RNSPoly::RNSPoly(ContextData& context, const std::vector<std::vector<uint64_t>>& data)
    70	    : RNSPoly(context, data.size() - 1) {
    71	
    72	    assert(data.size() <= cc.prime.size());
    73	    std::vector<uint64_t> moduli(data.size());
    74	    for (size_t i = 0; i < data.size(); ++i)
    75	        moduli[i] = cc.prime[i].p;
    76	    load(data, moduli);
    77	}
    78	
    79	RNSPoly::RNSPoly(RNSPoly&& src) noexcept
    80	    : uid(src.uid), cc(src.cc), level(src.level), modUp(src.modUp), GPU(std::move(src.GPU)) {
    81	    for (auto& g : GPU) {
    82	        g.level = &(this->level);
    83	    }
    84	    //src.setLevel(-2);
    85	}

    87	int RNSPoly::getLevel() const {
    88	    return level;
    89	}

    91	void RNSPoly::freeSpecialLimbs() {
    92	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
    93	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
    94	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
    95	        GPU.at(i).freeSpecialLimbs();
    96	    }
    97	    this->SetModUp(false);
    98	}
    99	
   100	void RNSPoly::generateSpecialLimbs(const bool zero_out, const bool for_communication) {
   101	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   102	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   103	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   104	        GPU[i].generateSpecialLimb(zero_out, for_communication);
   105	    }
   106	}

   108	void RNSPoly::generateDecompAndDigit(bool iskey) {
   109	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   110	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   111	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   112	        GPU[i].generateAllDecompAndDigit(iskey);
   113	    }
   114	}

   116	void RNSPoly::loadDecompDigit(const std::vector<std::vector<std::vector<uint64_t>>>& data,
   117	                              const std::vector<std::vector<uint64_t>>& moduli) {
   118	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   119	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   120	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   121	        GPU.at(i).loadDecompDigit(data, moduli);
   122	    }
   123	}
   124	
   125	void RNSPoly::store(std::vector<std::vector<uint64_t>>& data) {
   126	    data.resize(level + 1);
   127	    for (size_t i = 0; i < data.size(); ++i) {
   128	        //auto& rec = cc.meta[cc.limbGPUid[i].x][cc.limbGPUid[i].y];
   129	        cudaSetDevice(GPU[cc.limbGPUid[i].x].device);
   130	        SWITCH(GPU[cc.limbGPUid[i].x].limb[cc.limbGPUid[i].y], store_convert(data[i]));
   131	    }
   132	}

   134	bool RNSPoly::isModUp() const {
   135	    return modUp;
   136	}
   137	void RNSPoly::SetModUp(bool newValue) {
   138	    modUp = newValue;
   139	}
   140	void RNSPoly::scaleByP() {
   141	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   142	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   143	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   144	        GPU.at(i).scaleByP();
   145	    }
   146	    this->SetModUp(true);
   147	}
   148	void RNSPoly::multNoModdownEnd(RNSPoly& c0, const RNSPoly& bc0, const RNSPoly& bc1, const RNSPoly& in,
   149	                               const RNSPoly& aux) {
   150	    assert(in.isModUp());
   151	    assert(aux.isModUp());
   152	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   153	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   154	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   155	        GPU.at(i).multNoModdownEnd(c0.GPU.at(i), bc0.GPU.at(i), bc1.GPU.at(i), in.GPU.at(i), aux.GPU.at(i));
   156	    }
   157	    this->SetModUp(true);
   158	    c0.SetModUp(true);
   159	}
   160	
   161	void RNSPoly::binomialMult(RNSPoly& c1, RNSPoly& in, const RNSPoly& d0, const RNSPoly& d1, bool moddown, bool square) {
   162	    assert(!this->isModUp() && !c1.isModUp() && !d0.isModUp() && !d1.isModUp());
   163	
   164	    if (!moddown) {
   165	        this->generateSpecialLimbs(true, false);
   166	        CudaCheckErrorMod;
   167	        c1.generateSpecialLimbs(true, false);
   168	    }
   169	
   170	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   171	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   172	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   173	        GPU.at(i).binomialMult(c1.GPU.at(i), in.GPU.at(i), d0.GPU.at(i), d1.GPU.at(i), !moddown, square);
   174	    }
   175	    this->SetModUp(!moddown);
   176	    c1.SetModUp(!moddown);
   177	    in.SetModUp(!moddown);
   178	}
   179	
   180	void RNSPoly::add(const RNSPoly& p) {
   181	
   182	    if (p.isModUp() && !this->isModUp()) {
   183	        //std::cout << "Adapt non modup destination add" << std::endl;
   184	        generateSpecialLimbs(true, false);
   185	        scaleByP();
   186	    }
   187	    assert(p.isModUp() == this->isModUp());
   188	    assert(level <= p.level);
   189	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   190	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   191	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   192	        GPU.at(i).add(p.GPU.at(i), this->isModUp() || p.isModUp());
   193	    }
   194	    this->SetModUp(this->isModUp() || p.isModUp());
   195	}
   196	
   197	void RNSPoly::sub(const RNSPoly& p) {
   198	    assert(level <= p.level);
   199	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   200	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   201	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   202	        GPU.at(i).sub(p.GPU.at(i));
   203	    }
   204	}
   205	
   206	void RNSPoly::modup() {
   207	    //  assert(GPU.size() == 1 || 0 == "ModUp Multi-GPU not implemented.");
   208	    RNSPoly& aux = cc.getKeySwitchAux2();
   209	
   210	    std::vector<std::atomic_uint64_t> thread_stop_buffer(cc.GPUid.size() * 8);
   211	    std::vector<std::atomic_uint64_t*> thread_stop(cc.GPUid.size(), nullptr);
   212	    for (int k = 0; k < cc.GPUid.size(); ++k) {
   213	        thread_stop[k] = &thread_stop_buffer[8 * k];
   214	        thread_stop_buffer[8 * k] = 0;
   215	    }
   216	
   217	    std::vector<Stream*> external_s;
   218	    for (int i = 0; i < GPU.size(); ++i) {
   219	        external_s.push_back(&GPU[i].s);
   220	    }
   221	
   222	    std::vector<uint64_t*> buffergather;
   223	    for (int i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   224	        buffergather.push_back(GPU.at(i).bufferGATHER);
   225	    }
   226	    if (cc.GPUid.size() == 1) {
   227	        for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   228	            GPU.at(i).modupMGPU(aux.GPU.at(i), buffergather, thread_stop, external_s);
   229	        }
   230	    } else {
   231	#pragma omp parallel num_threads(GPU.size())
   232	        {
   233	            int i = omp_get_thread_num();
   234	
   235	            if (omp_get_num_threads() != (int)GPU.size())
   236	                throw std::invalid_argument("OMP didn't create enough threads");
   237	            assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)GPU.size());
   238	            assert(i < GPU.size());
   239	            GPU.at(i).modupMGPU(aux.GPU.at(i), buffergather, thread_stop, external_s);
   240	        }
   241	    }
   242	}
   243	
   244	void RNSPoly::sync() {
   245	    for (auto& i : GPU) {
   246	        for (auto& j : i.limb) {
   247	            assert(STREAM(j).ptr() != nullptr);
   248	            cudaStreamSynchronize(STREAM(j).ptr());
   249	        }
   250	        cudaStreamSynchronize(i.s.ptr());
   251	    }
   252	}
   253	
   254	void RNSPoly::rescale() {
   255	    //    assert(GPU.size() == 1 && "Rescale Multi-GPU not implemented.");
   256	    if (GPU.size() == 1) {
   257	        for (auto& i : GPU) {
   258	            i.rescale();
   259	        }
   260	        level -= 1;
   261	    } else {
   262	        int more_than_0 = 0;
   263	        for (size_t i = 0; i < GPU.size(); ++i)
   264	            if (GPU[i].getLimbSize(level) != 0)
   265	                more_than_0++;
   266	
   267	        if (more_than_0 == 1) {
   268	            for (auto& i : GPU) {
   269	                if (i.getLimbSize(level) > 0)
   270	                    i.rescale();
   271	            }
   272	        } else {
   273	#pragma omp parallel num_threads(GPU.size())
   274	            {
   275	#pragma omp for
   276	                for (size_t i = 0; i < GPU.size(); ++i) {
   277	                    if (omp_get_num_threads() != (int)GPU.size())
   278	                        throw std::invalid_argument("OMP didn't create enough threads");
   279	                    assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)GPU.size());
   280	                    GPU[i].rescaleMGPU();
   281	                }
   282	            }
   283	        }
   284	        level -= 1;
   285	    }
   286	}
   287	
   288	void RNSPoly::rescaleDouble(RNSPoly& poly) {
   289	    //    assert(GPU.size() == 1 && "Rescale Multi-GPU not implemented.");
   290	    if (0 && GPU.size() == 1) {
   291	        for (auto& i : GPU) {
   292	            i.rescale();
   293	        }
   294	        level -= 1;
   295	        for (auto& i : poly.GPU) {
   296	            i.rescale();
   297	        }
   298	        poly.level -= 1;
   299	    } else {
   300	
   301	        int more_than_0 = 0;
   302	        for (size_t i = 0; i < GPU.size(); ++i)
   303	            if (GPU[i].getLimbSize(level) > 0)
   304	                more_than_0++;
   305	
   306	        if (0 && more_than_0 == 1) {
   307	            for (size_t i = 0; i < GPU.size(); ++i) {
   308	                if (GPU[i].getLimbSize(level) > 0) {
   309	                    GPU[i].rescale();
   310	                    poly.GPU[i].rescale();
   311	                }
   312	            }
   313	        } else {
   314	
   315	            if (0 && MEMCPY_PEER) {
   316	
   317	                int id = cc.limbGPUid[level].x;
   318	                GPU[id].doubleRescaleMGPU(poly.GPU[id]);
   319	                for (size_t i = 0; i < GPU.size(); ++i) {
   320	
   321	                    // if (omp_get_num_threads() != (int)GPU.size())
   322	                    //     throw std::invalid_argument("OMP didn't create enough threads");
   323	                    // assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)GPU.size());
   324	                    //GPU[i].rescaleMGPU();
   325	                    if (i != id)
   326	                        GPU[i].doubleRescaleMGPU(poly.GPU[i]);
   327	                }
   328	            } else {
   329	#pragma omp parallel num_threads(GPU.size())
   330	                {
   331	                    int i = omp_get_thread_num();
   332	
   333	                    if (omp_get_num_threads() != (int)GPU.size())
   334	                        throw std::invalid_argument("OMP didn't create enough threads");
   335	                    assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)GPU.size());
   336	                    assert(i < GPU.size());
   337	                    //GPU[i].rescaleMGPU();
   338	                    GPU[i].doubleRescaleMGPU(poly.GPU[i]);
   339	                }
   340	            }
   341	            level -= 1;
   342	            poly.level -= 1;
   343	        }
   344	    }
   345	}
   346	
   347	void RNSPoly::multPt(const RNSPoly& p, bool rescale) {
   348	    if (rescale) {
   349	        if (GPU.size() == 1) {
   350	            for (size_t i = 0; i < GPU.size(); ++i) {
   351	                GPU.at(i).multPt(p.GPU.at(i));
   352	            }
   353	            --level;
   354	        } else {
   355	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(GPU.size())
   356	            for (size_t i = 0; i < GPU.size(); ++i) {
   357	                assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)GPU.size());
   358	                GPU.at(i).multElement(p.GPU.at(i));
   359	                GPU.at(i).rescaleMGPU();
   360	            }
   361	            --level;
   362	        }
   363	    } else {
   364	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   365	        for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   366	            assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   367	            GPU.at(i).multElement(p.GPU.at(i));
   368	        }
   369	    }
   370	}
   371	
   372	template <ALGO algo>
   373	void RNSPoly::NTT(int batch, bool sync) {
   374	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   375	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   376	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   377	        GPU.at(i).NTT<algo>(batch, sync);
   378	    }
   379	}
   380	
   381	#define YY(algo) template void RNSPoly::NTT<algo>(int batch, bool sync);
   382	
   383	#include "ntt_types.inc"
   384	
   385	#undef YY
   386	
   387	template <ALGO algo>
   388	void RNSPoly::INTT(int batch, bool sync) {
   389	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   390	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   391	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   392	        GPU.at(i).INTT<algo>(batch, sync);
   393	    }
   394	}

   397	
   398	#include "ntt_types.inc"
   399	
   400	#undef YY

   402	/*
   403	std::array<RNSPoly, 2> RNSPoly::dotKSK(const KeySwitchingKey& ksk) {
   404	    constexpr bool PRINT = false;
   405	    Out(KEYSWITCH, "dotKSK in");
   406	
   407	    std::array<RNSPoly, 2> result{RNSPoly(cc, level, true), RNSPoly(cc, level, true)};
   408	    result[0].generateSpecialLimbs(false);
   409	    result[1].generateSpecialLimbs(false);
   410	
   411	    if constexpr (PRINT)
   412	        for (auto& i : ksk.b.GPU) {
   413	            for (auto& j : i.DECOMPlimb) {
   414	                for (auto& k : j) {
   415	                    SWITCH(k, printThisLimb(1));
   416	                }
   417	            }
   418	
   419	            for (auto& j : i.DIGITlimb) {
   420	                for (auto& k : j) {
   421	                    SWITCH(k, printThisLimb(1));
   422	                }
   423	            }
   424	        }
   425	    for (size_t i = 0; i < GPU.size(); ++i) {
   426	        dotKSKinto(result[0], ksk.b, level);
   427	        dotKSKinto(result[1], ksk.a, level);
   428	    }
   429	
   430	    Out(KEYSWITCH, "dotKSK out");
   431	    return result;
   432	}
   433	*/
   434	
   435	void RNSPoly::multElement(const RNSPoly& poly) {
   436	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   437	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   438	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   439	        GPU.at(i).multElement(poly.GPU.at(i));
   440	    }
   441	}
   442	
   443	void RNSPoly::multElement(const RNSPoly& poly1, const RNSPoly& poly2) {
   444	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   445	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   446	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   447	        GPU.at(i).multElement(poly1.GPU.at(i), poly2.GPU.at(i));
   448	    }
   449	}
   450	
   451	void RNSPoly::mult1AddMult23Add4(const RNSPoly& poly1, const RNSPoly& poly2, const RNSPoly& poly3,
   452	                                 const RNSPoly& poly4) {
   453	
   454	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   455	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   456	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   457	        GPU.at(i).mult1AddMult23Add4(poly1.GPU.at(i), poly2.GPU.at(i), poly3.GPU.at(i), poly4.GPU.at(i));
   458	    }
   459	}
   460	
   461	void RNSPoly::mult1Add2(const RNSPoly& poly1, const RNSPoly& poly2) {
   462	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   463	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   464	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   465	        GPU.at(i).mult1Add2(poly1.GPU.at(i), poly2.GPU.at(i));
   466	    }
   467	}
   468	
   469	void RNSPoly::dotKSKinto(RNSPoly& acc, const RNSPoly& ksk, const RNSPoly* limbsrc) {
   470	#pragma omp parallel for num_threads(cc.GPUid.size())
   471	    for (size_t i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   472	        assert(omp_get_num_threads() == (int)cc.GPUid.size());
   473	        acc.GPU.at(i).dotKSK(GPU.at(i), ksk.GPU.at(i), false, limbsrc ? &limbsrc->GPU.at(i) : nullptr);
   474	    }
   475	}
   476	
   477	void RNSPoly::multModupDotKSK(RNSPoly& c1, const RNSPoly& c1tilde, RNSPoly& c0, const RNSPoly& c0tilde,
   478	                              const KeySwitchingKey& key) {
   479	    assert(GPU.size() == 1 && "multModupDotKSK Multi-GPU not implemented.");
   480	    assert(c1.level <= c1tilde.level);
   481	    if (cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTO || cc.rescaleTechnique == FLEXIBLEAUTOEXT) {
   482	        assert(level == c1.level);
   483	        assert(level == c1tilde.level);
   484	        assert(level == c0.level);
   485	        assert(level == c0tilde.level);
   486	    }
   487	    generateDecompAndDigit(false);
   488	    c0.generateSpecialLimbs(false, false);
   489	    c1.generateSpecialLimbs(false, false);
   490	    for (size_t i = 0; i < GPU.size(); ++i) {
   491	        GPU.at(i).multModupDotKSK(c1.GPU.at(i), c1tilde.GPU.at(i), c0.GPU.at(i), c0tilde.GPU.at(i), key.a.GPU.at(i),
   492	                                  key.b.GPU.at(i));
   493	    }
   494	    c0.SetModUp(true);
   495	    c1.SetModUp(true);
   496	}
   497	
   498	void RNSPoly::rotateModupDotKSK(RNSPoly& c0, RNSPoly& c1, const KeySwitchingKey& key) {
   499	    assert(GPU.size() == 1 && "rotateModupDotKSK Multi-GPU not implemented.");
   500	    generateDecompAndDigit(false);
   501	    c0.generateSpecialLimbs(false, false);
   502	    c1.generateSpecialLimbs(false, false);
   503	    for (size_t i = 0; i < GPU.size(); ++i) {
   504	        GPU.at(i).rotateModupDotKSK(c1.GPU.at(i), c0.GPU.at(i), key.a.GPU.at(i), key.b.GPU.at(i));
   505	    }
   506	    c1.SetModUp(true);
   507	    c0.SetModUp(true);
   508	}
   509	
   510	template <ALGO algo>
   511	void RNSPoly::moddown(bool ntt, bool free, int aux_num) {
   512	    if (!this->isModUp()) {
   513	        std::cout << "RNSPoly calling MOdDown on non-modup polynomial." << std::endl;
   514	    }
   515	    assert(this->isModUp());
   516	
   517	    if (cc.GPUid.size() == 1) {
   518	        for (int i = 0; i < (int)GPU.size(); ++i) {
   519	            GPU.at(i).moddown<algo>(cc.getModdownAux(aux_num).GPU.at(i), ntt, free);
   520	        }

    14	template <typename T>
    15	Limb<T>::Limb(Limb<T>&& l) noexcept
    16	    : cc(l.cc), primeid(l.primeid), stream(l.stream), v(std::move(l.v)), aux(std::move(l.aux)), id(l.id), raw(l.raw) {}
    17	
    18	template <typename T>
    19	Limb<T>::~Limb() noexcept {
    20	    v.free(stream);
    21	    aux.free(stream);
    22	}
    23	
    24	template <typename T>
    25	Limb<T>::Limb(ContextData& context, const int id, Stream& stream, const int primeid, bool constant)
    26	    : cc(context),
    27	      primeid(primeid),
    28	      stream(stream /*StartStream(primeid, cc.L + cc.K + 1)*/),
    29	      v(stream, context.N, cc.GPUid[id]),
    30	      aux(stream, constant ? 0 : context.N, cc.GPUid[id]),
    31	      id(id),
    32	      raw(!cc.isValidPrimeId(primeid)) {
    33	    // TODO: CryptoContext limb tracking.
    34	    //id = cc.generateId(this);
    35	    if (raw) {
    36	        assert(primeid == -1);
    37	    }
    38	    // assert(stream.ptr() != nullptr);
    39	    // assert(stream.ev != nullptr);
    40	    int dev;
    41	    cudaGetDevice(&dev);
    42	    assert(this->v.size == cc.N);
    43	    assert(dev == v.device);
    44	}
    45	
    46	/**
    47	     * Caution! Auxiliar vector is not managed and operations like INTT and NTT shouldn't be used on this.
    48	     * TODO add assertions for correct use.
    49	     */
    50	template <typename T>
    51	Limb<T>::Limb(ContextData& context, T* data, const int offset, const int id, Stream& stream, const int primeid,
    52	              T* data_aux, const int offset_aux)
    53	    : cc(context),
    54	      primeid(primeid),
    55	      stream(stream /*StartStream(primeid, cc.L + cc.K + 1)*/),
    56	      v(data, context.N, cc.GPUid[id], offset),
    57	      aux(data_aux ? data_aux : data, context.N, cc.GPUid[id], data_aux ? offset_aux : offset),
    58	      id(id),
    59	      raw(!cc.isValidPrimeId(primeid)) {
    60	    // TODO: CryptoContext limb tracking.
    61	    //id = cc.generateId(this);
    62	    if (raw) {
    63	        assert(primeid == -1);
    64	    }
    65	    // assert(stream.ptr() != nullptr);
    66	    // assert(stream.ev != nullptr);
    67	
    68	    int dev;
    69	    cudaGetDevice(&dev);
    70	    assert(this->v.size == cc.N);
    71	    assert(dev == v.device);
    72	}

    76	    return cc.precom.globals->globals[id];

    79	template <typename T>
    80	void Limb<T>::store(std::vector<T>& dat) const {
    81	    dat.resize(v.size);
    82	
    83	    //cudaHostRegister((void*)dat.data(), dat.size() * sizeof(T), cudaHostRegisterDefault);
    84	    //cudaMemcpyAsync((void *) dat.data(), v.data, dat.size() * sizeof(T), cudaMemcpyDeviceToHost, stream.ptr());
    85	
    86	    cudaMemcpyAsync((void*)dat.data(), v.data, dat.size() * sizeof(T), cudaMemcpyDeviceToHost, stream.ptr());
    87	    cudaStreamSynchronize(stream.ptr());
    88	    //cudaDeviceSynchronize();
    89	    //cudaHostUnregister((void*)dat.data());
    90	}
    91	
    92	template <typename T>
    93	template <typename Q>
    94	void Limb<T>::load(const std::vector<Q>& dat_) {
    95	    assert(dat_.size() <= v.size);
    96	    int device = -1;
    97	    cudaGetDevice(&device);
    98	    // std::cout << v.device << " " << device << ",";
    99	    std::vector<T> dat;
   100	    if constexpr (!std::is_same<T, Q>().value) {
   101	        dat.assign(v.size, 0);
   102	        for (size_t i = 0; i < dat.size(); ++i) {
   103	            dat[i] = dat_[i];
   104	        }
   105	    } else {
   106	        dat = dat_;
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    //cudaHostRegister((void *) dat.data(), dat.size() * sizeof(T), cudaHostRegisterDefault);
   110	    //cudaDeviceSynchronize();
   111	    cudaMemcpyAsync(v.data, dat.data(), dat.size() * sizeof(T), cudaMemcpyHostToDevice, stream.ptr());
   112	    //cudaDeviceSynchronize();
   113	    //cudaHostUnregister((void *) dat.data());
   114	}

   129	template <typename T>
   130	template <typename Q>
   131	void Limb<T>::load_convert(const std::vector<Q>& dat_raw) {
   132	    assert(dat_raw.size() <= v.size);
   133	    std::vector<T> dat(dat_raw.size());
   134	
   135	    for (size_t i = 0; i < dat.size(); ++i)
   136	        dat[i] = static_cast<T>(dat_raw[i]);
   137	
   138	    load(dat);
   139	}

   145	template <typename T>
   146	template <typename Q>
   147	void Limb<T>::store_convert(std::vector<Q>& dat_raw) {
   148	    dat_raw.resize(v.size);
   149	    if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, Q>) {
   150	        store(dat_raw);
   151	    } else {
   152	        std::vector<T> dat(v.size);
   153	        store(dat);
   154	        for (size_t i = 0; i < dat.size(); ++i)
   155	            dat_raw[i] = static_cast<Q>(dat[i]);
   156	    }
   157	}

   163	template <typename T>
   164	void Limb<T>::add(const LimbImpl& l) {
   165	    switch (l.index()) {
   166	        case U32:
   167	            add(std::get<U32>(l));
   168	            break;
   169	        case U64:
   170	            add(std::get<U64>(l));
   171	            break;
   172	    }
   173	}

   175	template <>
   176	void Limb<uint64_t>::add(const Limb<uint64_t>& l) {
   177	    //stream.wait(l.stream);
   178	    dim3 blockDim{block};
   179	    dim3 gridDim{(uint32_t)(cc.N) / block};
   180	    add_<uint64_t><<<gridDim, blockDim, 0, stream.ptr()>>>(v.data, l.v.data, primeid);
   181	}

   258	    assert(v.size == l.v.size);
   259	    mult_<uint32_t, ALGO_BARRETT><<<v.size / block, block, 0, stream.ptr()>>>(v.data, l.v.data, primeid);
   260	}

   268	void Limb<uint64_t>::mult(const Limb<uint64_t>& l) {
   269	    assert(v.size == l.v.size);
   270	    mult_<uint64_t, ALGO_BARRETT><<<v.size / block, block, 0, stream.ptr()>>>(v.data, l.v.data, primeid);
   271	}
   272	
   273	template <>
   274	void Limb<uint64_t>::mult(const LimbImpl& _l1, const LimbImpl& _l2, const bool inplace) {
   275	    assert(_l1.index() == U64);
   276	    assert(_l2.index() == U64);
   277	    using T = uint64_t;
   278	    const Limb<T>& l1 = std::get<U64>(_l1);
   279	    const Limb<T>& l2 = std::get<U64>(_l2);
   280	
   281	    mult_<T, ALGO_BARRETT>
   282	        <<<v.size / block, block, 0, stream.ptr()>>>(inplace ? aux.data : v.data, l1.v.data, l2.v.data, primeid);
   283	}
   284	
   285	template <>
   286	void Limb<uint32_t>::mult(const LimbImpl& _l1, const LimbImpl& _l2, const bool inplace) {
   287	    assert(_l1.index() == U32);
   288	    assert(_l2.index() == U32);
   289	    using T = uint32_t;
   290	    const Limb<T>& l1 = std::get<U32>(_l1);
   291	    const Limb<T>& l2 = std::get<U32>(_l2);
   292	
   293	    mult_<T, ALGO_BARRETT>
   294	        <<<v.size / block, block, 0, stream.ptr()>>>(inplace ? aux.data : v.data, l1.v.data, l2.v.data, primeid);
   295	}
   296	
   297	template <typename T>
   298	template <ALGO algo>
   299	void Limb<T>::INTT() {
   300	    assert(primeid >= 0);
   301	    constexpr int M = sizeof(T) == 8 ? 4 : 8;
   302	
   303	    if constexpr (1) {
   304	        dim3 blockDim = 1 << ((cc.logN) / 2 - 1);
   305	        dim3 gridDim{v.size / blockDim.x / 2 / M};
   306	        int bytes = sizeof(T) * blockDim.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == 3 ? 1 : 0));
   307	
   308	        INTT_<T, false, algo><<<gridDim, blockDim, bytes, stream.ptr()>>>(getGlobals(), v.data, primeid, aux.data);
   309	
   310	        blockDim = (1 << ((cc.logN + 1) / 2 - 1));
   311	        gridDim = {v.size / blockDim.x / 2 / M};
   312	        bytes = sizeof(T) * blockDim.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == 3 ? 1 : 0));
   313	
   314	        INTT_<T, true, algo><<<gridDim, blockDim, bytes, stream.ptr()>>>(getGlobals(), aux.data, primeid, v.data);
   315	    }
   316	}
   317	
   318	template <typename T>
   319	template <ALGO algo>
   320	void Limb<T>::NTT() {
   321	
   322	    if constexpr (0) {
   323	        assert(primeid >= 0);
   324	        constexpr int M = sizeof(T) == 8 ? 4 : 8;
   325	        constexpr int K = 1;
   326	
   327	        dim3 blockDim{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN + 1) / 2 - 1)), K};
   328	        dim3 gridDim{v.size / blockDim.x / 2 / M};
   329	        int bytes = sizeof(T) * blockDim.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == 3 ? 1 : 0));
   330	
   331	        //T *psi_arr = (T *) G_::psi[primeid];
   332	        //T *psi_arr_middle_scale = (T *) G_::psi_middle_scale[primeid];
   333	
   334	        int primeid_ = primeid;
   335	        void* args[6] = {getGlobals(), &v.data, (void*)&primeid_, &aux.data, (void*)&primeid_, (void*)&primeid_};
   336	        cudaLaunchCooperativeKernel(get_NTT_reference(false) /*(void *) test_kernel*/ /*(void *) NTT_<T, false, algo>*/,
   337	                                    gridDim, blockDim, args, bytes, stream.ptr());
   338	        //CudaCheckErrorModNoSync;
   339	    } else if constexpr (1) {
   340	        static std::map<int, cudaGraphExec_t> exec;
   341	
   342	        run_in_graph<false>(exec[primeid], stream, [&]() {
   343	            assert(primeid >= 0);
   344	            constexpr int M = sizeof(T) == 8 ? 4 : 8;
   345	
   346	            dim3 blockDim{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN + 1 + (cc.logN > 13 ? 0 : 0)) / 2 - 1))};
   347	            dim3 gridDim{v.size / blockDim.x / 2 / M};
   348	            int bytes = sizeof(T) * blockDim.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == 3 ? 1 : 0));
   349	
   350	            NTT_<T, false, algo><<<gridDim, blockDim, bytes, stream.ptr()>>>(getGlobals(), v.data, primeid, aux.data);
   351	
   352	            {
   353	                blockDim = dim3{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN + (cc.logN > 13 ? 0 : 0)) / 2 - 1))};
   354	                gridDim = {v.size / blockDim.x / 2 / M};
   355	                bytes = sizeof(T) * blockDim.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == 3 ? 1 : 0));
   356	
   357	                NTT_<T, true, algo>
   358	                    <<<gridDim, blockDim, bytes, stream.ptr()>>>(getGlobals(), aux.data, primeid, v.data);
   359	            }
   360	        });
   361	
   362	        //aux.free(stream);
   363	    }
   364	}
   365	
   366	template <>
   367	void Limb<uint64_t>::NTT_rescale_fused(const Limb<uint64_t>& l) {
   368	
   369	    constexpr ALGO algo = ALGO_SHOUP;
   370	    using T = uint64_t;
   371	    constexpr int M = sizeof(T) == 8 ? 4 : 8;
   372	
   373	    assert(primeid >= 0);
   374	    assert(l.primeid >= 0);
   375	
   376	    dim3 blockDim{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN + 1) / 2 - 1))};
   377	    dim3 gridDim{v.size / blockDim.x / 2 / M};
   378	    int bytes = sizeof(T) * blockDim.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == 3 ? 1 : 0));
   379	
   380	    NTT_<T, false, algo, NTT_RESCALE>
   381	        <<<gridDim, blockDim, bytes, stream.ptr()>>>(getGlobals(), l.v.data, primeid, aux.data, nullptr, l.primeid);
   382	    blockDim = (1 << ((cc.logN) / 2 - 1));
   383	    gridDim = {v.size / blockDim.x / 2 / M};
   384	    bytes = sizeof(T) * blockDim.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == 3 ? 1 : 0));
   385	
   386	    NTT_<T, true, algo, NTT_RESCALE>
   387	        <<<gridDim, blockDim, bytes, stream.ptr()>>>(getGlobals(), aux.data, primeid, v.data, nullptr, l.primeid);
   388	}
   389	
   390	template <>
   391	void Limb<uint32_t>::NTT_rescale_fused(const Limb<uint32_t>& l) {
   392	    assert("Not implemented." == nullptr);
   393	}
   394	
   395	template <>
   396	void Limb<uint64_t>::NTT_rescale_fused(const Limb<uint32_t>& l) {
   397	    assert("Not implemented." == nullptr);
   398	}
   399	
   400	template <>
   401	void Limb<uint32_t>::NTT_rescale_fused(const Limb<uint64_t>& l) {
   402	    assert("Not implemented." == nullptr);
   403	}
   404	
   405	template <typename T>
   406	void Limb<T>::NTT_rescale_fused(const LimbImpl& l) {
   407	    switch (l.index()) {
   408	        case U32:
   409	            NTT_rescale_fused(std::get<U32>(l));
   410	            break;
   411	        case U64:
   412	            NTT_rescale_fused(std::get<U64>(l));
   413	            break;
   414	    }
   415	}
   416	
   417	template <>
   418	void Limb<uint64_t>::NTT_moddown_fused(const LimbImpl& _l) {
   419	    assert(_l.index() == U64);
   420	    using T = uint64_t;

    53	      SPECIALlimbptr(std::move(l.SPECIALlimbptr)),
    54	      SPECIALauxptr(std::move(l.SPECIALauxptr)),
    55	      DECOMPlimbptr(std::move(l.DECOMPlimbptr)),
    56	      //      DECOMPauxptr(std::move(l.DECOMPlimbptr)),
    57	      DIGITlimbptr(std::move(l.DIGITlimbptr)),
    58	      //      DIGITauxptr(std::move(l.DIGITlimbptr)),
    59	      GATHERptr(std::move(l.GATHERptr)),
    60	      bufferDECOMPandDIGIT(l.bufferDECOMPandDIGIT),
    61	      bufferSPECIAL(l.bufferSPECIAL),
    62	      bufferLIMB(l.bufferLIMB),
    63	      bufferGATHER(l.bufferGATHER),
    64	      bufferDECOMPandDIGIT_handle(l.bufferDECOMPandDIGIT_handle),
    65	      bufferGATHER_handle(l.bufferGATHER_handle) {
    66	    l.bufferSPECIAL = nullptr;
    67	    l.bufferLIMB = nullptr;
    68	    l.bufferDECOMPandDIGIT = nullptr;
    69	    l.bufferAUXptrs = nullptr;
    70	    l.bufferGATHER = nullptr;
    71	    l.bufferDECOMPandDIGIT_handle = nullptr;
    72	    l.bufferGATHER_handle = nullptr;
    73	}
    74	
    75	std::vector<VectorGPU<void*>> LimbPartition::generateDecompLimbptr(
    76	    void** buffer, const std::vector<std::vector<LimbRecord>>& DECOMPmeta, const int device, int offset) {
    77	    std::vector<VectorGPU<void*>> result;
    78	    for (auto& d : DECOMPmeta) {
    79	        result.emplace_back(buffer, std::max(1ul, d.size()), device, offset);
    80	        offset += MAXP;
    81	    }
    82	    return result;
    83	}
    84	
    85	void** CudaMallocAuxBuffer(Stream& stream, unsigned long size, int device) {
    86	    void** malloc;
    87	    CudaCheckErrorModNoSync;
    88	    malloc = (void**)GPUmalloc(device, MAXP * sizeof(void*) * (4ul + 4 * std::max(size, 1ul)), stream.ptr(), false);
    89	    //cudaMallocAsync(&malloc, MAXP * sizeof(void*) * (4ul + 4 * std::max(size, 1ul)),
    90	    //                stream.ptr());  // TODO: can reduce to 3
    91	    CudaCheckErrorModNoSync;
    92	    return malloc;
    93	}
    94	
    95	Stream initStream(bool default_) {
    96	    Stream s;
    97	    if (default_) {
    98	        s.initDefault();
    99	    } else {
   100	        s.init(50);
   101	    }
   102	    return s;
   103	}

   105	LimbPartition::LimbPartition(ContextData& cc, const uint64_t& uid, int* level, const int id, const bool def_stream)
   106	    : cc(cc),
   107	      uid(uid),
   108	      level(level),
   109	      id(id),
   110	      device((cudaSetDevice(cc.GPUid.at(id)), cc.GPUid.at(id))),
   111	      rank(cc.GPUrank.at(id)),
   112	      s(initStream(def_stream)),
   113	      meta(cc.meta.at(id)),
   114	      SPECIALmeta(cc.specialMeta.at(id)),
   115	      digitid(cc.GPUdigits.at(id)),
   116	      DECOMPmeta(cc.decompMeta.at(id)),
   117	      DIGITmeta(cc.digitMeta.at(id)),
   118	      GATHERmeta(cc.gatherMeta),
   119	      DECOMPlimb(DECOMPmeta.size()),
   120	      DIGITlimb(DIGITmeta.size()),
   121	      bufferAUXptrs(CudaMallocAuxBuffer(s, cc.dnum, device)),
   122	      /*
   123	            limbptr(s, meta.size(), device),
   124	            auxptr(s, meta.size(), device),
   125	            SPECIALlimbptr(s, SPECIALmeta.size(), device),
   126	            SPECIALauxptr(s, SPECIALmeta.size(), device),
   127	            */
   128	
   129	      limbptr(bufferAUXptrs, std::max(1ul, meta.size()), device, 0),
   130	      auxptr(bufferAUXptrs, std::max(1ul, meta.size()), device, MAXP),
   131	      SPECIALlimbptr(bufferAUXptrs, std::max(1ul, SPECIALmeta.size()), device, 2 * MAXP),
   132	      SPECIALauxptr(bufferAUXptrs, std::max(1ul, SPECIALmeta.size()), device, 3 * MAXP),
   133	
   134	      DECOMPlimbptr(generateDecompLimbptr(bufferAUXptrs, DECOMPmeta, device, 4 * MAXP)),
   135	      //      DECOMPauxptr(generateDecompLimbptr(bufferAUXptrs, DECOMPmeta, device, (4 + DECOMPmeta.size()) * MAXP)),
   136	      DIGITlimbptr(generateDecompLimbptr(bufferAUXptrs, DIGITmeta, device, (4 + DECOMPmeta.size()) * MAXP)),
   137	      //      , DIGITauxptr(generateDecompLimbptr(bufferAUXptrs, DIGITmeta, device, (4 + 3 * DECOMPmeta.size()) * MAXP))
   138	      GATHERptr(bufferAUXptrs, std::max(1ul, GATHERmeta.size()), device, (4 + 2 * DECOMPmeta.size()) * MAXP) {}
   139	
   140	LimbPartition::~LimbPartition() {
   141	    CudaNvtxRange r(std::string{sc::current().function_name()}.substr());
   142	    cudaSetDevice(device);
   143	    /*
   144	        for (auto &i: limb) s.wait(STREAM(i));
   145	        for (auto &i: SPECIALlimb) s.wait(STREAM(i));
   146	        for (auto &i: DECOMPlimb) for (auto &j: i) s.wait(STREAM(j));
   147	        for (auto &i: DIGITlimb) for (auto &j: i) s.wait(STREAM(j));
   148	*/
   149	
   150	    limbptr.free(s);
   151	    auxptr.free(s);
   152	    SPECIALlimbptr.free(s);
   153	    SPECIALauxptr.free(s);
   154	    GATHERptr.free(s);
   155	    for (auto& d : DECOMPlimbptr)
   156	        d.free(s);
   157	    //    for (auto& d : DECOMPauxptr)
   158	    //        d.free(s);
   159	    for (auto& d : DIGITlimbptr)
   160	        d.free(s);
   161	    // for (auto& d : DIGITauxptr)
   162	    //    d.free(s);
   163	
   164	    //CudaCheckErrorMod;
   165	    if (bufferDECOMPandDIGIT_handle) {
   166	        cudaStreamSynchronize(s.ptr());
   167	#ifdef NCCL
   168	        if (bufferDECOMPandDIGIT_handle != (void*)-1)
   169	            NCCLCHECK(ncclCommDeregister(rank, bufferDECOMPandDIGIT_handle));
   170	        NCCLCHECK(ncclMemFree(bufferDECOMPandDIGIT));
   171	#else
   172	        assert(false);
   173	#endif
   174	    } else {
   175	        if (bufferDECOMPandDIGIT)
   176	            GPUfree(bufferDECOMPandDIGIT, id, 0, s.ptr());
   177	        // cudaFreeAsync(bufferDECOMPandDIGIT, s.ptr());
   178	    }
   179	    if (bufferSPECIAL)
   180	        GPUfree(bufferSPECIAL, id, 0, s.ptr());
   181	    //cudaFreeAsync(bufferSPECIAL, s.ptr());
   182	    if (bufferLIMB) {
   183	        GPUfree(bufferLIMB, id, 0, s.ptr());
   184	        //cudaFreeAsync(bufferLIMB, s.ptr());
   185	    }
   186	    if (bufferAUXptrs)
   187	        GPUfree(bufferAUXptrs, id, MAXP * sizeof(void*) * (4ul + 4 * std::max(cc.dnum, 1)), s.ptr(), false);
   188	    // cudaFreeAsync(bufferAUXptrs, s.ptr());
   189	    if (bufferGATHER_handle) {
   190	        cudaStreamSynchronize(s.ptr());
   191	
   192	#ifdef NCCL
   193	        if (bufferGATHER_handle != (void*)-1)
   194	            NCCLCHECK(ncclCommDeregister(rank, bufferGATHER_handle));
   195	        NCCLCHECK(ncclMemFree(bufferGATHER));
   196	#else
   197	        assert(false);
   198	#endif
   199	    } else {
   200	        if (bufferGATHER)
   201	            GPUfree(bufferGATHER, id, 0, s.ptr());
   202	        //cudaFreeAsync(bufferGATHER, s.ptr());
   203	    }
   204	    limb.clear();
   205	    SPECIALlimb.clear();
   206	    DECOMPlimb.clear();
   207	    DIGITlimb.clear();
   208	}

   210	Global::Globals* LimbPartition::getGlobals() {
   211	    return cc.precom.globals->globals[id];
   212	}
   213	
   214	void LimbPartition::generate(std::vector<LimbRecord>& records, std::vector<LimbImpl>& limbs, VectorGPU<void*>& ptrs,
   215	                             int pos, VectorGPU<void*>* auxptrs, uint64_t* buffer, size_t offset, uint64_t* buffer_aux,
   216	                             size_t offset_aux, bool noptr) {
   217	    CudaNvtxRange r(std::string{sc::current().function_name()}.substr());
   218	    constexpr bool USE_PARTITION_STREAM = true;
   219	    assert(pos < (int)records.size());
   220	    cudaSetDevice(device);
   221	
   222	    const int limbs_size = limbs.size();
   223	    int size = std::max((int)(pos - limbs_size + 1), (int)0);
   224	    std::vector<void*> cpu_ptr(size, nullptr);
   225	    std::vector<void*> cpu_auxptr(size, nullptr);
   226	    for (int i = limbs_size; i <= pos; ++i) {
   227	        const LimbRecord& r = records.at(i);
   228	        if (r.type == U32) {
   229	            if (buffer && buffer_aux) {
   230	                limbs.emplace_back(Limb<uint32_t>(cc, (uint32_t*)buffer, 2 * offset, id,
   231	                                                  USE_PARTITION_STREAM ? s : records.at(i).stream, r.id,
   232	                                                  (uint32_t*)buffer_aux, 2 * offset_aux));
   233	                offset += cc.N;
   234	                offset_aux += cc.N;
   235	            } else if (buffer) {
   236	                limbs.emplace_back(Limb<uint32_t>(cc, (uint32_t*)buffer, 2 * offset, id,
   237	                                                  USE_PARTITION_STREAM ? s : records.at(i).stream, r.id, nullptr, 0));
   238	                offset += cc.N;
   239	            } else
   240	                limbs.emplace_back(
   241	                    Limb<uint32_t>(cc, id, USE_PARTITION_STREAM ? s : records.at(i).stream, r.id, auxptrs ? 1 : 0));
   242	            cpu_ptr[i - limbs_size] = {&(std::get<U32>(limbs.back()).v.data)[0]};
   243	            cpu_auxptr[i - limbs_size] = {&(std::get<U32>(limbs.back()).aux.data)[0]};
   244	        }
   245	        if (r.type == U64) {
   246	            if (buffer && buffer_aux) {
   247	                limbs.emplace_back(Limb<uint64_t>(cc, buffer, offset, id,
   248	                                                  USE_PARTITION_STREAM ? s : records.at(i).stream, r.id, buffer_aux,
   249	                                                  offset_aux));
   250	                offset += cc.N;
   251	                offset_aux += cc.N;
   252	            } else if (buffer) {
   253	                limbs.emplace_back(Limb<uint64_t>(cc, buffer, offset, id,
   254	                                                  USE_PARTITION_STREAM ? s : records.at(i).stream, r.id, nullptr, 0));
   255	                offset += cc.N;
   256	            } else {
   257	                if (auxptrs) {
   258	                    limbs.emplace_back(
   259	                        Limb<uint64_t>(cc, id, USE_PARTITION_STREAM ? s : records.at(i).stream, r.id, false));
   260	                } else {
   261	                    limbs.emplace_back(
   262	                        Limb<uint64_t>(cc, id, USE_PARTITION_STREAM ? s : records.at(i).stream, r.id, true));
   263	                }
   264	            }
   265	
   266	            cpu_ptr[i - limbs_size] = {&(std::get<U64>(limbs.back()).v.data)[0]};
   267	            cpu_auxptr[i - limbs_size] = {&(std::get<U64>(limbs.back()).aux.data)[0]};
   268	            //cudaFreeHost(aux);
   269	        }
   270	        CudaCheckErrorModNoSync;
   271	        s.wait(USE_PARTITION_STREAM ? s : records.at(i).stream);
   272	        CudaCheckErrorModNoSync;
   273	    }
   274	    if (size > 0) {
   275	        if (!noptr) {
   276	            cudaMemcpyAsync(ptrs.data + limbs_size, cpu_ptr.data(), size * sizeof(void*), cudaMemcpyHostToDevice,
   277	                            s.ptr());
   278	            CudaCheckErrorModNoSync;
   279	            if (auxptrs) {
   280	                cudaMemcpyAsync((*auxptrs).data + limbs_size, cpu_auxptr.data(), size * sizeof(void*),
   281	                                cudaMemcpyHostToDevice, s.ptr());
   282	            }
   283	            CudaCheckErrorModNoSync;
   284	        }
   285	    }
   286	    CudaCheckErrorModNoSync;
   287	}

   291	    generate(meta, limb, limbptr, (int)limb.size(), &auxptr);
   292	}
   293	*/
   294	
   295	void LimbPartition::generateLimbToLevel(int new_level) {
   296	    cudaSetDevice(device);
   297	    int new_size = getLimbSize(new_level);
   298	    if (new_size > limb.size()) {
   299	        generate(meta, limb, limbptr, new_size - 1, &auxptr);
   300	    }
   301	}

   320	        generate(DIGITmeta[i], DIGITlimb[i], DIGITlimbptr[i], (int)DIGITmeta[i].size() - 1, nullptr /*&DIGITauxptr[i]*/,
   321	                 pInt, offset, nullptr, 0);
   322	        offset += cc.N * DIGITmeta.at(i).size();
   323	    }
