   326	void LimbPartition::generateSpecialLimb(const bool zero_out, const bool for_communication) {
   327	    cudaSetDevice(device);
   328	    if ((for_communication && cc.GPUid.size() > 0 && bufferSPECIAL == nullptr && SPECIALmeta.size() > 0) ||
   329	        (!(for_communication && cc.GPUid.size() > 0) && SPECIALlimb.size() == 0 && SPECIALmeta.size() > 0)) {
   330	        if ((for_communication && cc.GPUid.size() > 0)) {
   331	            assert(SPECIALlimb.size() == 0);
   332	            cudaMalloc(&bufferSPECIAL, std::max(1ul, cc.N * SPECIALmeta.size() * 2 * sizeof(uint64_t)));
   333	            generate(SPECIALmeta, SPECIALlimb, SPECIALlimbptr, (int)SPECIALmeta.size() - 1, &SPECIALauxptr,
   334	                     bufferSPECIAL, 0, bufferSPECIAL, cc.N * SPECIALmeta.size());
   335	        } else {
   336	            assert(bufferSPECIAL == nullptr);
   337	            bufferSPECIAL = (uint64_t*)GPUmalloc(device, cc.N * SPECIALmeta.size() * 2 * sizeof(uint64_t), s.ptr());
   338	            CudaCheckErrorModNoSync;
   339	            //generate(SPECIALmeta, SPECIALlimb, SPECIALlimbptr, (int)SPECIALmeta.size() - 1, &SPECIALauxptr, nullptr, 0,
   340	            //         nullptr, 0);
   341	            //cudaMalloc(&bufferSPECIAL, std::max(1ul, cc.N * SPECIALmeta.size() * 2 * sizeof(uint64_t)));
   342	            generate(SPECIALmeta, SPECIALlimb, SPECIALlimbptr, (int)SPECIALmeta.size() - 1, &SPECIALauxptr,
   343	                     bufferSPECIAL, 0, bufferSPECIAL, cc.N * SPECIALmeta.size());
   344	
   345	            //cudaMallocAsync(&bufferDECOMPandDIGIT, cc.N * SPECIALmeta.size() * 2 * sizeof(uint64_t), s.ptr());
   346	        }
   347	    }
   348	    if (zero_out) {
   349	        if (bufferSPECIAL) {
   350	            if (cc.N * SPECIALmeta.size() * sizeof(uint64_t) > 0)
   351	                cudaMemsetAsync(bufferSPECIAL, 0, cc.N * SPECIALmeta.size() * sizeof(uint64_t), s.ptr());
   352	        } else {
   353	            for (auto& i : SPECIALlimb) {
   354	                if (i.index() == U32) {
   355	                    cudaMemsetAsync(std::get<U32>(i).v.data, 0, cc.N * sizeof(uint32_t), STREAM(i).ptr());
   356	                } else {
   357	                    cudaMemsetAsync(std::get<U64>(i).v.data, 0, cc.N * sizeof(uint64_t), STREAM(i).ptr());
   358	                }
   359	            }
   360	        }
   361	    }
   362	}
   363	
   364	template <ALGO algo, NTT_MODE mode>
   365	void LimbPartition::ApplyNTT(int batch, LimbPartition::NTT_fusion_fields fields, std::vector<LimbImpl>& limb,
   366	                             VectorGPU<void*>& limbptr, VectorGPU<void*>& auxptr, ContextData& cc,
   367	                             const int primeid_init, const int limbsize) {
   368	    constexpr int M = 4;
   369	
   370	    const dim3 blockDimFirst{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN + 1) / 2 - 1))};
   371	    const dim3 blockDimSecond = dim3{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN) / 2 - 1))};
   372	    const int bytesFirst = 8 * blockDimFirst.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == ALGO_SHOUP ? 1 : 0));
   373	    const int bytesSecond = 8 * blockDimSecond.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == ALGO_SHOUP ? 1 : 0));
   374	    const int size = (limbsize != -1 ? limbsize : limb.size()) - (mode == NTT_RESCALE || mode == NTT_MULTPT);
   375	
   376	    for (int i = 0; i < size; i += batch) {
   377	        uint32_t num_limbs = std::min((uint32_t)batch, (uint32_t)(size - i));
   378	
   379	        NTT_<false, algo, mode><<<dim3{cc.N / (blockDimFirst.x * M * 2), num_limbs}, blockDimFirst, bytesFirst,
   380	                                  STREAM(limb.at(i)).ptr()>>>(
   381	            getGlobals(),
   382	            (mode == NTT_RESCALE || mode == NTT_MULTPT) ? limbptr.data + size
   383	            : (mode == NTT_MODDOWN)                     ? fields.op2->limbptr.data + i
   384	                                                        : limbptr.data + i,
   385	            primeid_init + i, auxptr.data + i, nullptr,
   386	            (mode == NTT_RESCALE || mode == NTT_MULTPT) ? PRIMEID(limb[size]) : 0, nullptr, nullptr);
   387	
   388	        NTT_<true, algo, mode><<<dim3{cc.N / (blockDimSecond.x * M * 2), num_limbs}, blockDimSecond, bytesSecond,
   389	                                 STREAM(limb.at(i)).ptr()>>>(
   390	            getGlobals(), auxptr.data + i, primeid_init + i, limbptr.data + i,
   391	            mode == NTT_MULTPT ? fields.pt->limbptr.data + i : nullptr,
   392	            (mode == NTT_RESCALE || mode == NTT_MULTPT) ? PRIMEID(limb[size]) : 0, nullptr, nullptr);
   393	    }
   394	}
   395	
   396	template <ALGO algo, NTT_MODE mode>
   397	void LimbPartition::NTT(int batch, bool sync, NTT_fusion_fields fields) {
   398	    cudaSetDevice(device);
   399	    int limbsize = getLimbSize(*level);
   400	
   401	    if (batch >= 1) {
   402	        if (limbsize > 0) {
   403	            if (sync) {
   404	                for (int i = 0; i < limbsize; i += batch) {
   405	                    STREAM(limb[i]).wait(s);
   406	                }
   407	            }
   408	            ApplyNTT<algo, mode>(batch, fields, limb, limbptr, auxptr, cc, PARTITION(id, 0), limbsize);
   409	            if (sync) {
   410	                for (int i = 0; i < limbsize; i += batch) {
   411	                    s.wait(STREAM(limb[i]));
   412	                }
   413	            }
   414	        }
   415	    } else {
   416	        assert("Invalid NTT batch configuration!");
   417	    }
   418	}
   419	
   420	#define YYY(algo, mode) template void LimbPartition::NTT<algo, mode>(int batch, bool sync, NTT_fusion_fields fields);

    14	static bool envMemcopyPeer(bool def = false) {
    15	    bool out = def;
    16	
    17	    char* res = getenv("FIDESLIB_USE_MEMCPY_PEER");
    18	    if (res && !(0 == std::strcmp(res, ""))) {
    19	        out = atoi(res);
    20	        std::cout << "FIDESLIB_USE_MEMCPY_PEER=" << res << ", set to: " << out << std::endl;
    21	        /*
    22	        if ((res == "0" || res == "false" || res == "False" || res == "FALSE")) {
    23	            std::cout << "Use memcpy peer deactivated" << std::endl;
    24	            out = false;
    25	        }
    26	
    27	        if ((res == "1" || res == "true" || res == "True" || res == "TRUE")) {
    28	            std::cout << "Use memcpy peer activated" << std::endl;
    29	            out = true;
    30	        }
    31	        */
    32	    }
    33	    return out;
    34	}

    37	    bool out = def;
    38	
    39	    char* res = getenv("FIDESLIB_USE_GRAPH_CAPTURE");
    40	    if (res && !(0 == std::strcmp(res, ""))) {
    41	        out = atoi(res);
    42	        std::cout << "FIDESLIB_USE_GRAPH_CAPTURE=" << res << ", set to: " << out << std::endl;
    43	        /*
    44	        if ((res == "0" || res == "false" || res == "False" || res == "FALSE")) {
    45	            std::cout << "Use memcpy peer deactivated" << std::endl;
    46	            out = false;
    47	        }
    48	
    49	        if ((res == "1" || res == "true" || res == "True" || res == "TRUE")) {
    50	            std::cout << "Use memcpy peer activated" << std::endl;
    51	            out = true;
    52	        }
    53	        */
    54	    }
    55	    return out;
    56	}

    58	bool MEMCPY_PEER = envMemcopyPeer(true);
    59	bool GRAPH_CAPTURE = envGraphCapture(false);
    60	
    61	void LimbPartition::rescaleMGPU() {
    62	    const int limbsize = getLimbSize(*level);
    63	    cudaSetDevice(device);
    64	
    65	    Stream& stream = cc.top_limb_stream[id];
    66	    uint64_t* buffer = cc.top_limb_buffer[id];
    67	    VectorGPU<void*>& ptr = cc.top_limbptr[id];
    68	
    69	    if (cc.limbGPUid[*level].x == id) {
    70	        if (limb.size() > cc.limbGPUid[*level].y && PRIMEID(limb[cc.limbGPUid[*level].y]) == *level) {
    71	
    72	            LimbImpl& top = limb.at(limbsize - 1);
    73	            stream.wait(s);
    74	            //SWITCH(top, INTT<ALGO_SHOUP>());
    75	            {
    76	                constexpr ALGO algo = ALGO_SHOUP;
    77	                constexpr int M = 4;
    78	
    79	                dim3 blockDimFirst{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN) / 2 - 1))};
    80	                dim3 blockDimSecond = dim3{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN + 1) / 2 - 1))};
    81	                int bytesFirst = 8 * blockDimFirst.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == 3 ? 1 : 0));
    82	                int bytesSecond = 8 * blockDimSecond.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == 3 ? 1 : 0));
    83	
    84	                int start = 0;
    85	                for (int i = limbsize - 1; i < limbsize; i += cc.batch) {
    86	                    cc.top_limb_stream.at(id).wait(s);
    87	                    uint32_t num_limbs = 1;
    88	
    89	                    INTT_<false, algo, INTT_NONE>
    90	                        <<<dim3{cc.N / (blockDimFirst.x * M * 2), num_limbs}, blockDimFirst, bytesFirst,
    91	                           stream.ptr()>>>(getGlobals(), limbptr.data + start + i, PARTITION(id, start + i),
    92	                                           cc.top_limbptr.at(cc.GPUid.size() + id).data);
    93	                    INTT_<true, algo, INTT_NONE>
    94	                        <<<dim3{cc.N / (blockDimSecond.x * M * 2), num_limbs}, blockDimSecond, bytesSecond,
    95	                           stream.ptr()>>>(getGlobals(), cc.top_limbptr.at(cc.GPUid.size() + id).data,
    96	                                           PARTITION(id, start + i), cc.top_limbptr.at(id).data);
    97	                }
    98	                //s.wait(cc.top_limb_stream.at(id));
    99	            }
   100	            //STREAM(top).wait(stream);
   101	            //cudaMemcpyAsync(buffer, std::get<U64>(top).v.data, cc.N * sizeof(uint64_t), cudaMemcpyDeviceToDevice,
   102	            //                STREAM(top).ptr());
   103	            //stream.wait(STREAM(top));
   104	            /*
   105	            std::cout << "GPU: " << id << " ";
   106	            SWITCH(top, printThisLimb(2));
   107	            std::cout << std::endl;
   108	*/
   109	            //while (bufferLIMB == nullptr && limb.size() > limbsize - 1) {
   110	            //    STREAM(limb.back()).wait(stream);
   111	            //    limb.pop_back();
   112	            //}
   113	        } else {
   114	            std::cout << "Cant find the top limb!!!" << id << " " << *level << " " << cc.limbGPUid[*level].y << " "
   115	                      << limb.size() << std::endl;
   116	        }
   117	    } else {
   118	        //stream.wait(s);
   119	    }
   120	
   121	    if (cc.GPUid.size() > 1) {
   122	        if (MEMCPY_PEER && cc.canP2P) {
   123	
   124	            int top_gpu = cc.limbGPUid[*level].x;
   125	            if (top_gpu == id)
   126	                stream.record();
   127	
   128	            openmp_synchronize();
   129	
   130	            if (top_gpu != id) {
   131	                for (int i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   132	                    if (i == id) {
   133	                        //cudaSetDevice(cc.GPUid[i]);
   134	                        stream.wait(cc.top_limb_stream[top_gpu]);
   135	                        cudaMemcpyPeerAsync(buffer, cc.GPUid[i], cc.top_limb_buffer[top_gpu], cc.GPUid[top_gpu],
   136	                                            cc.N * sizeof(uint64_t), stream.ptr());
   137	                    }
   138	                    CudaCheckErrorModNoSync;
   139	                }
   140	                cudaSetDevice(device);
   141	            }
   142	        } else {
   143	
   144	#ifdef NCCL
   145	            if constexpr (0) {
   146	                NCCLCHECK(ncclBroadcast(buffer, buffer, cc.N, ncclUint64, cc.limbGPUid[*level].x, rank, stream.ptr()));
   147	            } else {
   148	                NCCLCHECK(ncclGroupStart());
   149	                if (id == cc.limbGPUid[*level].x) {
   150	                    for (int i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   151	                        if (i != id)
   152	                            ncclSend(buffer, cc.N, ncclUint64, i, rank, stream.ptr());
   153	                    }
   154	                } else {
   155	                    ncclRecv(buffer, cc.N, ncclUint64, cc.limbGPUid[*level].x, rank, stream.ptr());
   156	                }
   157	                NCCLCHECK(ncclGroupEnd());
   158	            }
   159	#else
   160	            assert(false);
   161	#endif
   162	        }
   163	    }
   164	    /* {
   165	        std::vector<uint64_t> data(cc.N, 0);
   166	        cudaMemcpyAsync(data.data(), buffer, cc.N * sizeof(uint64_t), cudaMemcpyDeviceToHost, stream.ptr());
   167	        cudaDeviceSynchronize();
   168	        std::cout << "GPU " << id << " (" << data[0] << " " << data[1] << ")" << std::endl;
   169	    } */
   170	
   171	    {
   172	        {
   173	            stream.wait(s);
   174	            constexpr ALGO algo = ALGO_SHOUP;
   175	            constexpr int M = 4;
   176	
   177	            const dim3 blockDimFirst{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN + 1) / 2 - 1))};
   178	            const dim3 blockDimSecond = dim3{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN) / 2 - 1))};
   179	            const int bytesFirst = 8 * blockDimFirst.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == ALGO_SHOUP ? 1 : 0));
   180	            const int bytesSecond = 8 * blockDimSecond.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == ALGO_SHOUP ? 1 : 0));
   181	            const int size = getLimbSize(*level - 1);
   182	            const int batch = cc.batch;
   183	            const NTT_MODE mode = NTT_RESCALE;
   184	
   185	            for (int i = 0; i < size; i += batch) {
   186	                uint32_t num_limbs = std::min((uint32_t)batch, (uint32_t)(size - i));
   187	
   188	                NTT_<false, algo, mode>
   189	                    <<<dim3{cc.N / (blockDimFirst.x * M * 2), num_limbs}, blockDimFirst, bytesFirst, stream.ptr()>>>(
   190	                        getGlobals(), ptr.data, PARTITION(id, i), auxptr.data + i, nullptr, *level);
   191	
   192	                s.wait(stream);  // Data dependency on top_limb reaches only to here
   193	
   194	                NTT_<true, algo, mode>
   195	                    <<<dim3{cc.N / (blockDimSecond.x * M * 2), num_limbs}, blockDimSecond, bytesSecond, s.ptr()>>>(
   196	                        getGlobals(), auxptr.data + i, PARTITION(id, i), limbptr.data + i, nullptr, *level);
   197	            }
   198	        }
   199	    }
   200	    if (cc.GPUid.size() > 1) {
   201	        openmp_synchronize();
   202	        if (MEMCPY_PEER && cc.canP2P) {
   203	            if (cc.limbGPUid[*level].x == id) {
   204	                for (int i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   205	                    if (i != id) {
   206	                        stream.wait(cc.top_limb_stream[i]);
   207	                    }
   208	                }
   209	            }
   210	        }
   211	    }
   212	}
   213	
   214	void LimbPartition::doubleRescaleMGPU(LimbPartition& partition) {
   215	    const int limbsize = getLimbSize(*level);
   216	    assert(limbsize == getLimbSize(*partition.level));
   217	    cudaSetDevice(device);
   218	
   219	    Stream* stream[2] = {&cc.top_limb_stream[id], &cc.top_limb_stream2[id]};
   220	
   221	    uint64_t* buffer[2] = {cc.top_limb_buffer[id], cc.top_limb_buffer2[id]};
   222	
   223	    VectorGPU<void*>* ptr[2] = {&cc.top_limbptr[id], &cc.top_limbptr2[id]};
   224	    VectorGPU<void*>* ptraux[2] = {&cc.top_limbptr[cc.GPUid.size() + id], &cc.top_limbptr2[cc.GPUid.size() + id]};
   225	
   226	    LimbPartition* part[2] = {this, &partition};
   227	    //parity = !parity;
   228	
   229	    for (int i = 0; i < 2; ++i) {
   230	        if (cc.limbGPUid[*part[i]->level].x == id) {
   231	            if (part[i]->limb.size() > cc.limbGPUid[*part[i]->level].y &&
   232	                PRIMEID(part[i]->limb[cc.limbGPUid[*part[i]->level].y]) == *part[i]->level) {
   233	                LimbImpl& top = part[i]->limb.at(limbsize - 1);
   234	                if (1) {
   235	                    stream[i]->wait(part[i]->s);
   236	                    constexpr ALGO algo = ALGO_SHOUP;
   237	                    constexpr int M = 4;
   238	
   239	                    dim3 blockDimFirst{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN) / 2 - 1))};
   240	                    dim3 blockDimSecond = dim3{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN + 1) / 2 - 1))};
   241	                    int bytesFirst = 8 * blockDimFirst.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == 3 ? 1 : 0));
   242	                    int bytesSecond = 8 * blockDimSecond.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == 3 ? 1 : 0));
   243	
   244	                    int start = 0;
   245	                    for (int i_ = limbsize - 1; i_ < limbsize; i_ += cc.batch) {
   246	                        //stream[i]->wait(i ? partition.s : s);
   247	                        uint32_t num_limbs = 1;
   248	
   249	                        INTT_<false, algo, INTT_NONE>
   250	                            <<<dim3{cc.N / (blockDimFirst.x * M * 2), num_limbs}, blockDimFirst, bytesFirst,
   251	                               stream[i]->ptr()>>>(getGlobals(), part[i]->limbptr.data + start + i_,
   252	                                                   PARTITION(id, start + i_), ptraux[i]->data);
   253	                        INTT_<true, algo, INTT_NONE><<<dim3{cc.N / (blockDimSecond.x * M * 2), num_limbs},
   254	                                                       blockDimSecond, bytesSecond, stream[i]->ptr()>>>(
   255	                            getGlobals(), ptraux[i]->data, PARTITION(id, start + i_), ptr[i]->data);
   256	                    }
   257	                    //s.wait(cc.top_limb_stream.at(id));
   258	                } else {
   259	                    STREAM(top).wait(part[i]->s);
   260	                    SWITCH(top, INTT<ALGO_SHOUP>());
   261	                    stream[i]->wait(STREAM(top));
   262	                    cudaMemcpyAsync(buffer[i], std::get<U64>(top).v.data, cc.N * sizeof(uint64_t),
   263	                                    cudaMemcpyDeviceToDevice, stream[i]->ptr());
   264	                }
   265	                /*
   266	            std::cout << "GPU: " << id << " ";
   267	            SWITCH(top, printThisLimb(2));
   268	            std::cout << std::endl;
   269	*/
   270	                //while (part[i]->bufferLIMB == nullptr && part[i]->limb.size() > limbsize - 1) {
   271	                //    STREAM(part[i]->limb.back()).wait(*stream[i]);
   272	                //    part[i]->limb.pop_back();
   273	                //}
   274	            } else {
   275	                std::cout << "Cant find the top limb!!!" << part[i]->id << " " << *part[i]->level << " "
   276	                          << cc.limbGPUid[*part[i]->level].y << " " << part[i]->limb.size() << std::endl;
   277	            }
   278	        } else {
   279	            stream[i]->wait(part[i]->s);
   280	            //stream[i]->record();
   281	        }
   282	    }
   283	
   284	    if (cc.GPUid.size() > 1) {
   285	        if (MEMCPY_PEER && cc.canP2P) {
   286	            //openmp_synchronize();
   287	
   288	            int top_gpu = cc.limbGPUid[*level].x;
   289	            if (top_gpu == id) {
   290	                stream[0]->record();
   291	                stream[1]->record();
   292	            }
   293	            openmp_synchronize();
   294	
   295	            if (top_gpu != id) {
   296	                for (int i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   297	
   298	                    if (i == id) {
   299	                        {
   300	                            // auto& stream_0 = cc.digitStreamForMemcpyPeer[0].at(id).at(i);
   301	                            // auto& stream_1 = cc.digitStreamForMemcpyPeer[cc.dnum > 1 ? 1 : 0].at(id).at(i);
   302	
   303	                            if (limbsize > 0) {
   304	                                stream[0]->wait(cc.top_limb_stream[top_gpu]);
   305	                                stream[1]->wait(cc.top_limb_stream2[top_gpu]);
   306	
   307	                                //stream_0.wait(cc.top_limb_stream[i]);
   308	                                //stream_1.wait(cc.top_limb_stream2[i]);
   309	                                cudaMemcpyPeerAsync(buffer[0], cc.GPUid[i], cc.top_limb_buffer[top_gpu],
   310	                                                    cc.GPUid[top_gpu], cc.N * sizeof(uint64_t), stream[0]->ptr());
   311	                                cudaMemcpyPeerAsync(buffer[1], cc.GPUid[i], cc.top_limb_buffer2[top_gpu],
   312	                                                    cc.GPUid[top_gpu], cc.N * sizeof(uint64_t), stream[1]->ptr());
   313	                            }
   314	                        }
   315	                    }
   316	                    CudaCheckErrorModNoSync;
   317	                }
   318	
   319	                cudaSetDevice(device);
   320	            }
   321	        } else {
   322	#ifdef NCCL
   323	            {
   324	                NCCLCHECK(ncclGroupStart());
   325	                if (id == cc.limbGPUid[*level].x) {
   326	                    for (int i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   327	                        if (i != id) {
   328	                            ncclSend(buffer[0], cc.N, ncclUint64, i, rank, stream[0]->ptr());
   329	                            ncclSend(buffer[1], cc.N, ncclUint64, i, rank, stream[1]->ptr());
   330	                        }
   331	                    }
   332	                } else {
   333	                    ncclRecv(buffer[0], cc.N, ncclUint64, cc.limbGPUid[*part[0]->level].x, rank, stream[0]->ptr());
   334	                    ncclRecv(buffer[1], cc.N, ncclUint64, cc.limbGPUid[*part[1]->level].x, rank, stream[1]->ptr());
   335	                }
   336	                NCCLCHECK(ncclGroupEnd());
   337	            }
   338	#else
   339	            assert(false);
   340	#endif
   341	        }
   342	        /* {
   343	            std::vector<uint64_t> data(cc.N, 0);
   344	            cudaMemcpyAsync(data.data(), buffer, cc.N * sizeof(uint64_t), cudaMemcpyDeviceToHost, stream.ptr());
   345	            cudaDeviceSynchronize();
   346	            std::cout << "GPU " << id << " (" << data[0] << " " << data[1] << ")" << std::endl;
   347	        } */
   348	    }
   349	    for (int j = 0; j < 2; ++j) {
   350	        stream[j]->wait(part[j]->s);
   351	        {
   352	            constexpr ALGO algo = ALGO_SHOUP;
   353	            constexpr int M = 4;
   354	
   355	            const dim3 blockDimFirst{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN + 1) / 2 - 1))};
   356	            const dim3 blockDimSecond = dim3{(uint32_t)(1 << ((cc.logN) / 2 - 1))};
   357	            const int bytesFirst = 8 * blockDimFirst.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == ALGO_SHOUP ? 1 : 0));
   358	            const int bytesSecond = 8 * blockDimSecond.x * (2 * M + 1 + (algo == 2 || algo == ALGO_SHOUP ? 1 : 0));
   359	            const int size = getLimbSize(*part[j]->level - 1);
   360	            const int batch = cc.batch;
   361	            const NTT_MODE mode = NTT_RESCALE;
   362	
   363	            for (int i = 0; i < size; i += batch) {
   364	                uint32_t num_limbs = std::min((uint32_t)batch, (uint32_t)(size - i));
   365	
   366	                NTT_<false, algo, mode><<<dim3{cc.N / (blockDimFirst.x * M * 2), num_limbs}, blockDimFirst, bytesFirst,
   367	                                          stream[j]->ptr()>>>(getGlobals(), ptr[j]->data, PARTITION(part[j]->id, i),
   368	                                                              part[j]->auxptr.data + i, nullptr, *part[j]->level);
   369	                part[j]->s.wait(*stream[j]);
   370	                NTT_<true, algo, mode>
   371	                    <<<dim3{cc.N / (blockDimSecond.x * M * 2), num_limbs}, blockDimSecond, bytesSecond,
   372	                       part[j]->s.ptr()>>>(getGlobals(), part[j]->auxptr.data + i, PARTITION(part[j]->id, i),
   373	                                           part[j]->limbptr.data + i, nullptr, *part[j]->level);
   374	            }
   375	        }
   376	    }
   377	
   378	    if (cc.GPUid.size() > 1) {
   379	        if (MEMCPY_PEER && cc.canP2P) {
   380	            openmp_synchronize();
   381	            if (cc.limbGPUid[*level].x == id) {
   382	                for (int i = 0; i < cc.GPUid.size(); ++i) {
   383	                    if (i != id) {
   384	                        {
   385	                            stream[0]->wait(cc.top_limb_stream[i]);
   386	                            stream[1]->wait(cc.top_limb_stream2[i]);
   387	                        }
   388	                    }
   389	                    CudaCheckErrorModNoSync;
   390	                }
   391	            }
   392	        }
   393	    }
   394	}  // namespace FIDESlib::CKKS

     1	//
     2	// Created by carlos on 6/03/24.
     3	//
     4	
     5	#ifndef FIDESLIB_VECTORGPU_CUH
     6	#define FIDESLIB_VECTORGPU_CUH
     7	#include <driver_types.h>
     8	#include <cassert>
     9	#include <type_traits>
    10	#include <vector>
    11	#include "CudaUtils.cuh"
    12	#include "LogUtil.hpp"
    13	#include "cuda.h"
    14	namespace FIDESlib {
    15	template <typename T>
    16	class VectorGPU {
    17	    static_assert(std::is_trivially_copyable_v<T>);
    18	    bool freeing;
    19	    bool managed;
    20	
    21	   public:
    22	    T* data;
    23	    const int size;
    24	    const int device;
    25	
    26	    VectorGPU(VectorGPU<T>&& v) noexcept;
    27	    /*
    28	        VectorGPU<T> &operator=(VectorGPU<T> && v) noexcept
    29	         {
    30	            freeing = v.freeing;
    31	            managed = v.managed;
    32	            data = v.data;
    33	            size = v.size;
    34	            device = v.device;
    35	            v.freeing = true;
    36	            return *this;
    37	        }
    38	*/
    39	    VectorGPU<T>& operator=(VectorGPU<T>& other) = delete;
    40	    VectorGPU<T>& operator=(const VectorGPU<T>& v) = delete;
    41	    VectorGPU(const VectorGPU<T>& v) = delete;
    42	    VectorGPU(T* data, const int size, const int device, const int offset = 0);
    43	    VectorGPU(Stream& stream, const int size, const int device, const T* src = nullptr);
    44	    void free(Stream& stream);
    45	    ~VectorGPU();
    46	};
    47	
    48	}  // namespace FIDESlib
    49	#endif  //FIDESLIB_VECTORGPU_CUH

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
/root/fideslib/src/VectorGPU.cu
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
     1	//
     2	// Created by carlosad on 2/05/24.
     3	//
     4	#include "VectorGPU.cuh"
     5	
     6	namespace FIDESlib {
     7	template <typename T>
     8	VectorGPU<T>::VectorGPU(VectorGPU<T>&& v) noexcept
     9	    : freeing(v.freeing), managed(v.managed), data(v.data), size(v.size), device(v.device) {
    10	    v.freeing = true;
    11	    v.managed = false;
    12	}
    13	
    14	template <typename T>
    15	VectorGPU<T>::VectorGPU(T* data, const int size, const int device, const int offset)
    16	    : data(data + offset), size(size), device(device), managed(false), freeing(true) {
    17	    assert(data != nullptr);
    18	    {
    19	        cudaPointerAttributes att{};
    20	        cudaPointerGetAttributes(&att, data);
    21	        assert(att.type == cudaMemoryTypeManaged || att.type == cudaMemoryTypeDevice);
    22	        assert(att.device == this->device);
    23	    }
    24	    CudaCheckErrorModNoSync;
    25	    assert(size > 0);
    26	
    27	    Out(MEMORY, "Unmanaged vector construct OK");
    28	}
    29	
    30	template <typename T>
    31	VectorGPU<T>::~VectorGPU() {
    32	    assert(freeing == true);
    33	    Out(MEMORY, "Vector destruct OK");
    34	}
    35	
    36	template <typename T>
    37	void VectorGPU<T>::free(Stream& stream) {
    38	    if (!managed) {
    39	        return;
    40	    }
    41	    assert(!freeing);
    42	    //cudaDeviceSynchronize();
    43	    GPUfree(data, device, sizeof(T) * size, stream.ptr(), true);
    44	    //cudaFreeAsync((void*)data, stream.ptr());
    45	    freeing = true;
    46	    Out(MEMORY, "Managed vector free OK");
    47	}
    48	
    49	template <typename T>
    50	VectorGPU<T>::VectorGPU(Stream& stream, const int size, const int device, const T* src)
    51	    : data(nullptr), size(size), device(device), freeing(false), managed(true) {
    52	    assert(device >= 0);
    53	    {
    54	        int device_count = -1;
    55	        assert(cudaGetDeviceCount(&device_count) == cudaSuccess);
    56	        assert(device < device_count);
    57	    }
    58	    {
    59	        int dev = -1;
    60	        assert(cudaGetDevice(&dev) == cudaSuccess);
    61	        assert(dev == device);
    62	        //cudaSetDevice(device);
    63	    }
    64	    int bytes = size * sizeof(T);
    65	
    66	    if (size == 0) {
    67	        managed = false;
    68	        freeing = true;
    69	    } else {
    70	        //cudaDeviceSynchronize();
    71	        data = (T*)GPUmalloc(device, bytes, stream.ptr(), true);
    72	        //cudaDeviceSynchronize();
    73	        //cudaMallocAsync(&data, bytes, stream.ptr());
    74	
    75	        if (src != nullptr) {
    76	            cudaMemcpyAsync(data, src, bytes, cudaMemcpyHostToDevice, stream.ptr());
    77	        }
    78	    }
    79	    Out(MEMORY, "Managed vector construct OK");
    80	}
    81	
    82	template class VectorGPU<int>;
    83	template class VectorGPU<void*>;
    84	template class VectorGPU<void**>;
    85	template class VectorGPU<uint32_t>;
    86	template class VectorGPU<uint64_t>;
    87	}  // namespace FIDESlib

     1	
     2	#ifndef __RAW_CIPHER_TEXT__
     3	#define __RAW_CIPHER_TEXT__

    10	
    11	namespace FIDESlib::CKKS {
    12	
    13	constexpr bool REVERSE = false;
    14	
    15	/*
    16	* The rawCipherText Class contains the basic information needed to hold a ciphertext, with pointers to data that can be contained on the GPU or main memory
    17	* This is stored in RNS/DCRT format
    18	*/
    19	struct RawCipherText {
    20	    // lbcrypto::CryptoContext<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly> & cc; // Original CryptoContext object from OpenFHE;
    21	    lbcrypto::Ciphertext<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly> originalCipherText;  // Original Ciphertext object from OpenFHE;
    22	    std::vector<std::vector<uint64_t>> sub_0;
    23	    //uint64_t* sub_0; // pointer to sub-ciphertext 0
    24	    std::vector<std::vector<uint64_t>> sub_1;  // pointer to sub-ciphertext 1
    25	    uint64_t* sub_2;                           // pointer to sub-ciphertext 1
    26	    std::vector<uint64_t> moduli;              // moduli for each limb
    27	    int numRes;     // number of residues of ciphertext, length of moduli array and first dimension of sub-ciphertexts
    28	    int N;          // length of each polynomial
    29	    Format format;  // current format of ciphertext, either coefficient or evaluation
    30	    double Noise;
    31	    int NoiseLevel;
    32	    int slots;
    33	    std::string keyid;
    34	    //GPUCKKS::Event e;
    35	};
    36	
    37	struct RawPlainText {
    38	    //  lbcrypto::CryptoContext<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly> & cc; // Original CryptoContext object from OpenFHE;
    39	    lbcrypto::Plaintext originalPlainText;  // Original Ciphertext object from OpenFHE;
    40	    std::vector<std::vector<uint64_t>> sub_0;
    41	    std::vector<uint64_t> moduli;  // moduli for each limb
    42	    int numRes;     // number of residues of ciphertext, length of moduli array and first dimension of sub-ciphertexts
    43	    int N;          // length of each polynomial
    44	    Format format;  // current format of ciphertext, either coefficient or evaluation
    45	    double Noise;
    46	    int slots;
    47	    int NoiseLevel;
    48	};

   136	/** Used in AddBootstrapPrecomputation */
   137	void AddBootstrapPlaintexts(lbcrypto::CryptoContext<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly> cc, int slots, FIDESlib::CKKS::Context& GPUcc_,
   138	                            FIDESlib::CKKS::BootstrapPrecomputation& result);

   141	std::vector<int> GetBootstrapIndexes(lbcrypto::CryptoContext<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly> cc, int slots,
   142	                                     FIDESlib::CKKS::BootstrapPrecomputation* result_);
   143

   145	void AddBootstrapPrecomputation(const lbcrypto::PublicKey<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly>& publicKey, int slots,
   146	                                FIDESlib::CKKS::Context& GPUcc_);
   147

   149	void AddBootstrapPrecomputation(lbcrypto::CryptoContext<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly> cc,
   150	                                const lbcrypto::KeyPair<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly>& keys, int slots,
   151	                                FIDESlib::CKKS::Context& GPUcc);

   154	 * Used in AddBootstrapPrecomputation
   155	 */
   156	void AddBootstrapKeys(const lbcrypto::PublicKey<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly>& publicKey, int slots,
   157	                      FIDESlib::CKKS::Context& GPUcc_);

   160	 * Client-side bootstrap setup: Keys for FIDESlib Bootstrap do not match OpenFHE's, be careful if you intend to run Bootstrap on CPU
   161	 *
   162	 * The code can be used to implement SSE and regular Boot on a regular non-FIDESlib OpenFHE installation with server-side FIDESlib.
   163	 */
   164	void GenBootstrapKeys(const lbcrypto::KeyPair<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly>& keys, int slots);

    12	
    13	/**
    14	* Converts a vector of polynomial limbs to a single flattened array
    15	*/
    16	std::vector<std::vector<uint64_t>> FIDESlib::CKKS::GetRawArray(
    17	    std::vector<lbcrypto::PolyImpl<lbcrypto::NativeVector>> polys) {
    18	    // total size is r * N
    19	    int numRes = polys.size();
    20	    int numElements = (polys[0].GetValues() /*.m_values*/).GetLength();
    21	
    22	    std::vector<std::vector<uint64_t>> flattened(numRes, std::vector<uint64_t>(numElements));
    23	
    24	    // Fill the array
    25	    for (int r = 0; r < numRes; ++r) {
    26	        for (int i = 0; i < numElements; i++) {
    27	            flattened[r][i] = (polys[r].GetValues() /*.m_values*/)[i].ConvertToInt();
    28	        }
    29	    }
    30	    return flattened;
    31	};
    32	
    33	/**
    34	* Gets the moduli from a vector of polynomial limbs and returns a single array
    35	*/
    36	static std::vector<uint64_t> GetModuli(std::vector<lbcrypto::PolyImpl<lbcrypto::NativeVector>> polys) {
    37	    int numRes = polys.size();
    38	    std::vector<uint64_t> moduli(numRes);
    39	    for (int r = 0; r < numRes; r++) {
    40	        moduli[r] = polys[r].GetModulus().ConvertToInt();
    41	    }
    42	    return moduli;
    43	};
    44	
    45	/**
    46	* Converts a ciphertext from openFHE into the RawCiphertext format
    47	*/
    48	FIDESlib::CKKS::RawCipherText FIDESlib::CKKS::GetRawCipherText(lbcrypto::CryptoContext<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly>& cc,
    49	                                                               lbcrypto::Ciphertext<DCRTPoly> ct, int REV) {
    50	    RawCipherText result;  //{ .cc = cc };
    51	    //result.originalCipherText=ct;
    52	    result.numRes = ct->GetElements()[0].GetAllElements().size();
    53	    result.N = ((ct->GetElements()[0].GetAllElements())[0].GetValues() /*.m_values*/).GetLength();
    54	    result.sub_0 = GetRawArray(ct->GetElements()[0].GetAllElements());
    55	    result.sub_1 = GetRawArray(ct->GetElements()[1].GetAllElements());
    56	
    57	    // We read (hopefully) in eval form, and OpenFHE should be bit_reversed, so REVERSE == 0.
    58	    // Changed the REV variable to an argument to the function.
    59	    // purpose: profiling Automorph kernel with both bit-reversed and normal order ciphertexts.
    60	    if (!REV) {
    61	        for (auto& i : result.sub_0)
    62	            bit_reverse_vector(i);
    63	        for (auto& i : result.sub_1)
    64	            bit_reverse_vector(i);
    65	    }
    66	    result.moduli = GetModuli(ct->GetElements()[0].GetAllElements());
    67	    result.format = ct->GetElements()[0].GetFormat();
    68	
    69	    result.Noise = ct->GetScalingFactor();       // m_scalingFactor;
    70	    result.NoiseLevel = ct->GetNoiseScaleDeg();  // m_noiseScaleDeg;
    71	    result.keyid = ct->GetKeyTag();              // keyTag;
    72	    result.slots = ct->GetSlots();
    73	
    74	    return result;
    75	};
    76	
    77	/**
    78	* Converts a ciphertext from the RawCiphertext format back to the OpenFHE ciphertext format*/
    79	void FIDESlib::CKKS::GetOpenFHECipherText(lbcrypto::Ciphertext<DCRTPoly> result, RawCipherText raw, int REV) {
    80	
    81	    int size = result->GetElements()[0].GetAllElements().size();
    82	    if (size < raw.numRes) {
    83	        raw.numRes = size;
    84	        raw.sub_0.resize(size);
    85	        raw.sub_1.resize(size);
    86	    }
    87	    assert(result->GetElements()[0].GetAllElements().size() >= raw.numRes);
    88	    // Changed the REV variable to an argument to the function.
    89	    // purpose: profiling Automorph kernel with both bit-reversed and normal order ciphertexts.
    90	    if (!REV) {
    91	        for (auto& i : raw.sub_0)
    92	            bit_reverse_vector(i);
    93	        for (auto& i : raw.sub_1)
    94	            bit_reverse_vector(i);
    95	    }
    96	    DCRTPoly sub_0 = result->GetElements().at(0);
    97	    DCRTPoly sub_1 = result->GetElements().at(1);
    98	    auto& dcrt_0 = sub_0.GetAllElements();
    99	    auto& dcrt_1 = sub_1.GetAllElements();
   100	    result->SetLevel(result->GetLevel() + result->GetElements().at(0).GetNumOfElements() - raw.numRes);
   101	    dcrt_0.resize(raw.numRes);
   102	    dcrt_1.resize(raw.numRes);
   103	    for (int r = 0; r < raw.numRes; r++) {
   104	        for (int i = 0; i < raw.N; i++) {
   105	            (*dcrt_0.at(r).m_values).at(i).SetValue(raw.sub_0.at(r).at(i));
   106	            (*dcrt_1.at(r).m_values).at(i).SetValue(raw.sub_1.at(r).at(i));
   107	        }
   108	    }
   109	
   110	    //sub_0.m_vectors=dcrt_0;
   111	    //sub_1.m_vectors=dcrt_1;
   112	    for (size_t i = sub_0.GetParams()->GetParams() /*m_params->m_params*/.size();
   113	         i > sub_0.GetAllElements() /*.m_vectors*/.size(); --i) {
   114	        DCRTPoly::Params* newP = new DCRTPoly::Params(*sub_0.GetParams() /*.m_params*/);
   115	        newP->PopLastParam();
   116	        sub_0.m_params.reset(newP);
   117	    }
   118	
   119	    for (size_t i = sub_1.GetParams()->GetParams().size(); i > sub_1.GetAllElements().size(); --i) {
   120	        DCRTPoly::Params* newP = new DCRTPoly::Params(*sub_1.GetParams());
   121	        newP->PopLastParam();
   122	        sub_1.m_params.reset(newP);
   123	    }
   124	
   125	    std::vector<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly> ct_new = {sub_0, sub_1};
   126	    result->SetElements(ct_new);
   127	
   128	    result->SetScalingFactor(raw.Noise);       // Getm_scalingFactor*/ = raw.Noise;
   129	    result->SetNoiseScaleDeg(raw.NoiseLevel);  // /*m_noiseScaleDeg*/ = raw.NoiseLevel;
   130	    result->SetKeyTag(raw.keyid);
   131	    result->SetSlots(raw.slots);
   132	}
   133	
   134	void FIDESlib::CKKS::GetOpenFHEPlaintext(lbcrypto::Plaintext result, RawPlainText raw, int REV) {
   135	
   136	    assert(result->GetElement<DCRTPoly>().GetAllElements().size() >= raw.numRes);
   137	    // Changed the REV variable to an argument to the function.
   138	    // purpose: profiling Automorph kernel with both bit-reversed and normal order ciphertexts.
   139	    if (!REV) {
   140	        for (auto& i : raw.sub_0)
   141	            bit_reverse_vector(i);
   142	    }
   143	    DCRTPoly sub_0 = result->GetElement<DCRTPoly>();
   144	    auto& dcrt_0 = sub_0.GetAllElements();
   145	    result->SetLevel(result->GetLevel() + result->GetElement<DCRTPoly>().GetNumOfElements() - raw.numRes);
   146	    dcrt_0.resize(raw.numRes);
   147	    for (int r = 0; r < raw.numRes; r++) {
   148	        for (int i = 0; i < raw.N; i++) {
   149	            (*dcrt_0.at(r).m_values).at(i).SetValue(raw.sub_0.at(r).at(i));
   150	        }
   151	    }
   152	
   153	    //sub_0.m_vectors=dcrt_0;
   154	    //sub_1.m_vectors=dcrt_1;
   155	    for (size_t i = sub_0.GetParams()->GetParams().size(); i > sub_0.GetAllElements().size(); --i) {
   156	        DCRTPoly::Params* newP = new DCRTPoly::Params(*sub_0.GetParams());
   157	        newP->PopLastParam();
   158	        sub_0.m_params.reset(newP);
   159	    }
   160	
   161	    result->GetElement<DCRTPoly>() /*encodedVectorDCRT*/ = sub_0;
   162	    result->SetScalingFactor(raw.Noise);       //scalingFactor = raw.Noise;
   163	    result->SetNoiseScaleDeg(raw.NoiseLevel);  // noiseScaleDeg = raw.NoiseLevel;
   164	    result->SetSlots(raw.slots);
   165	    /*
   166	    std::cout << result << std::endl;
   167	bool ok = result->Decode();
   168	    std::cout << ok << " " << result << std::endl;
   169	    */
   170	}
   171	
   172	FIDESlib::CKKS::RawPlainText FIDESlib::CKKS::GetRawPlainText(lbcrypto::CryptoContext<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly>& cc,
   173	                                                             lbcrypto::Plaintext pt) {
   174	    RawPlainText result;  //{.cc = cc};
   175	    result.originalPlainText = pt;
   176	    result.numRes = pt->GetElement<DCRTPoly>().GetAllElements().size();
   177	    result.N = ((pt->GetElement<DCRTPoly>().GetAllElements())[0].GetValues() /*.m_values*/).GetLength();
   178	    result.sub_0 = GetRawArray(pt->GetElement<DCRTPoly>().GetAllElements());
   179	    result.moduli = GetModuli(pt->GetElement<DCRTPoly>().GetAllElements());
   180	
   181	
   182	    result.format = pt->GetElement<DCRTPoly>().GetFormat();
   183	
   184	    if constexpr (REVERSE) {
   185	        for (auto& i : result.sub_0)
   186	            bit_reverse_vector(i);
   187	    }
   188	
   189	    result.Noise = pt->GetScalingFactor();
   190	    result.NoiseLevel = pt->GetNoiseScaleDeg();
   191	    result.slots = pt->GetSlots();
   192	
   193	    return result;
   194	}
   195	
   196	FIDESlib::CKKS::RawPlainText FIDESlib::CKKS::GetRawPlainText(lbcrypto::CryptoContext<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly>& cc,
   197	                                                             ReadOnlyPlaintext pt) {
   198	    RawPlainText result;  //{.cc = cc};
   199	    //result.originalPlainText = pt;
   200	    result.numRes = pt->GetElement<DCRTPoly>().GetAllElements().size();
   201	    result.N = ((pt->GetElement<DCRTPoly>().GetAllElements())[0].GetValues() /*.m_values*/).GetLength();
   202	    result.sub_0 = GetRawArray(pt->GetElement<DCRTPoly>().GetAllElements());
   203	    result.moduli = GetModuli(pt->GetElement<DCRTPoly>().GetAllElements());
   204	
   205	
   206	    result.format = pt->GetElement<DCRTPoly>().GetFormat();
   207	
   208	    if constexpr (REVERSE) {
   209	        for (auto& i : result.sub_0)
   210	            bit_reverse_vector(i);
   211	    }
   212	
   213	    result.Noise = pt->GetScalingFactor();
   214	    result.NoiseLevel = pt->GetNoiseScaleDeg();
   215	    result.slots = pt->GetSlots();
   216	
   217	    return result;
   218	}
   219	FIDESlib::CKKS::RawParams FIDESlib::CKKS::GetRawParams(lbcrypto::CryptoContext<lbcrypto::DCRTPoly> cc,
   220	                                                       FIDESlib::BOOT_CONFIG boot_conf) {
   221	    RawParams result;
   222	    result.N = cc->GetRingDimension();
   223	    result.logN = std::bit_width((uint32_t)result.N) - 1;
   224	    //cc->GetCryptoParameters()
   225	    result.L = cc->GetCryptoParameters()->GetElementParams()->GetParams().size() - 1;
   226	    //result.L = cc->params->m_params->m_params.size() - 1;
   227	    const auto cryptoParams = std::dynamic_pointer_cast<CryptoParametersCKKSRNS>(cc->GetCryptoParameters());
   228	    result.scalingTechnique = cryptoParams->GetScalingTechnique();
   229	    //result.qbit = cc->params->m_params->m_params->;
   230	    //auto aux = cc->GetCryptoParameters()->GetParamsPK()->GetParamPartition();
   231	
   232	    for (auto& i : /*cc->params->m_params->m_params*/
   233	         cc->GetCryptoParameters()->GetElementParams()->GetParams()) {
   234	        result.moduli.push_back(i->GetModulus().ConvertToInt<uint64_t>() /*m_ciphertextModulus.m_value*/);
   235	        result.root_of_unity.push_back(i->GetRootOfUnity().ConvertToInt<uint64_t>() /*m_rootOfUnity.m_value*/);
   236	        result.cyclotomic_order.push_back(i->GetCyclotomicOrder() /*m_cyclotomicOrder*/);
   237	    }
   238	
   239	    // intnat::ChineseRemainderTransformFTTNat<intnat::NativeVector>::m_rootOfUnityReverseTableByModulus
   240	    for (size_t i = 0; i < result.moduli.size(); ++i) {
   241	        using namespace intnat;
   242	        //  NumberTheoreticTransformNat<NativeVector>().PreCompute
   243	        using FFT = ChineseRemainderTransformFTTNat<NativeVector>;
   244	        auto mapSearch = FFT::m_rootOfUnityReverseTableByModulus.find(result.moduli[i]);
   245	        if (mapSearch == FFT::m_rootOfUnityReverseTableByModulus.end() ||
   246	            mapSearch->second.GetLength() != (size_t)result.N /*CycloOrderHf*/) {
   247	            FFT().PreCompute(result.root_of_unity[i], result.N << 1, result.moduli[i]);
   248	        }
   249	
   250	        if (mapSearch == FFT::m_rootOfUnityReverseTableByModulus.end() ||
   251	            mapSearch->second.GetLength() != (size_t)result.N /*CycloOrderHf*/) {
   252	            assert("OpenFHE has not generated the NTT tables we want yet :(" == nullptr);
   253	        }
   254	
   255	        {
   256	            int size = FFT::m_rootOfUnityReverseTableByModulus[result.moduli[i]].GetLength();
   257	
   258	            for (int k = 0; k < size; ++k) {
   259	                result.psi[i].push_back(FFT::m_rootOfUnityReverseTableByModulus[result.moduli[i]].at(k).ConvertToInt<uint64_t>() /*.m_value*/);
   260	                result.psi_inv[i].push_back(
   261	                    FFT::m_rootOfUnityInverseReverseTableByModulus[result.moduli[i]].at(k).ConvertToInt<uint64_t>() /*m_value*/);
   262	            }
   263	            result.N_inv.push_back(FFT::m_cycloOrderInverseTableByModulus.at(result.moduli[i]).at(result.logN).ConvertToInt<uint64_t>() /*.m_value*/);
   264	        }
   265	    }
   266	
   267	    //    intnat::NumberTheoreticTransformNat<intnat::NativeVector>().
   268	    //    mubintvec<ubint<unsigned long>>;
   269	
   270	    result.ModReduceFactor.resize(result.L + 1);
   271	    for (size_t i = 0; i < result.ModReduceFactor.size(); ++i) {
   272	        result.ModReduceFactor[/*result.L - */ i] = cryptoParams->GetModReduceFactor(i);
   273	    }
   274	    result.ScalingFactorReal.resize(result.L + 1);
   275	    for (size_t i = 0; i < result.ScalingFactorReal.size(); ++i) {
   276	        result.ScalingFactorReal[result.L - i] = cryptoParams->GetScalingFactorReal(i);
   277	    }
   278	
   279	    result.ScalingFactorRealBig.resize(result.L + 1);
   280	    for (size_t i = 0; i < result.ScalingFactorRealBig.size(); ++i) {
   281	        result.ScalingFactorRealBig[result.L - i] = cryptoParams->GetScalingFactorRealBig(i);
   282	    }
   283	
   284	    {
   285	        auto& src = cryptoParams->m_QlQlInvModqlDivqlModq;
   286	        auto& dest = result.m_QlQlInvModqlDivqlModq;
   287	        dest.resize(src.size());
   288	        for (size_t i = 0; i < src.size(); ++i) {
   289	            dest[i].resize(src[i].size());
   290	            for (size_t j = 0; j < src[i].size(); ++j) {
   291	                dest[i][j] = src[i][j].ConvertToInt<uint64_t>();
   292	            }
   293	        }
   294	    }
   295	
   296	    /// Key Switching precomputations !!!
   297	    result.dnum = cryptoParams->GetNumPartQ();
   298	    result.K = cryptoParams->GetParamsP()->GetParams().size();
   299	    assert(cryptoParams->GetNumPartQ() == cryptoParams->GetNumberOfQPartitions());
   300	    cryptoParams->GetNumPerPartQ();
   301	
   302	    {
   303	        auto& src = cryptoParams->GetParamsP()->m_params;
   304	        for (auto& i : src) {
   305	            result.SPECIALmoduli.push_back(i->GetModulus().ConvertToInt<uint64_t>() /* m_ciphertextModulus.m_value*/);
   306	            result.SPECIALroot_of_unity.push_back(
   307	                i->GetRootOfUnity().ConvertToInt<uint64_t>() /*m_rootOfUnity.m_value*/);
   308	            result.SPECIALcyclotomic_order.push_back(i->GetCyclotomicOrder() /*m_cyclotomicOrder*/);
   309	        }
   310	    }
   311	
   312	    {
   313	        auto& src = cryptoParams->m_paramsPartQ;
   314	        for (auto& i : src) {
   315	            result.PARTITIONmoduli.emplace_back();
   316	            for (auto& j : i->GetParams()) {
   317	                result.PARTITIONmoduli.back().push_back(
   318	                    j->GetModulus().ConvertToInt<uint64_t>() /*m_ciphertextModulus.m_value*/);
   319	            }
   320	        }
   321	    }
   322	
   323	    {
   324	        auto& src = cryptoParams->GetPHatInvModp();
   325	        auto& dest = result.PHatInvModp;
   326	        dest.resize(src.size());
   327	        for (size_t i = 0; i < src.size(); ++i) {
   328	            dest[i] = src[i].ConvertToInt<uint64_t>();
   329	        }
   330	    }
   331	
   332	    {
   333	        auto& src = cryptoParams->GetPInvModq();
   334	        auto& dest = result.PInvModq;
   335	        dest.resize(src.size());
   336	        for (size_t i = 0; i < src.size(); ++i) {
   337	            dest[i] = src[i].ConvertToInt<uint64_t>();  // m_value;
   338	        }
   339	    }
   340	
   341	    {
   342	        auto& src = cryptoParams->GetPHatModq();
   343	        auto& dest = result.PHatModq;
   344	        dest.resize(src.size());
   345	        for (size_t i = 0; i < src.size(); ++i) {
   346	            dest[i].resize(src[i].size());
   347	            for (size_t j = 0; j < src[i].size(); ++j) {
   348	                dest[i][j] = src[i][j].ConvertToInt<uint64_t>();  // m_value;
   349	            }
   350	        }
   351	    }
   352	
   353	    {
   354	        auto& dest = result.PartQlHatInvModq;
   355	        auto& src = cryptoParams->m_PartQlHatInvModq;
   356	        dest.resize(src.size());
   357	        for (size_t k = 0; k < dest.size(); ++k) {
   358	            dest[k].resize(src[k].size());
   359	            for (size_t i = 0; i < dest[k].size(); ++i) {
   360	                dest[k][i].resize(src[k][i].size());
   361	                for (size_t j = 0; j < src[k][i].size(); ++j) {
   362	                    dest[k][i][j] = src[k][i][j].ConvertToInt<uint64_t>();  // m_value;
   363	                }
   364	            }
   365	        }
   366	    }
   367	
   368	    {
   369	        auto& dest = result.PartQlHatModp;
   370	        auto& src = cryptoParams->m_PartQlHatModp;
   371	        dest.resize(result.dnum);
   372	        dest.resize(src.size());
   373	
   374	        for (size_t k = 0; k < dest.size(); ++k) {
   375	            dest[k].resize(src[k].size());
   376	            for (size_t i = 0; i < dest[k].size(); ++i) {
   377	                dest[k][i].resize(src[k][i].size());
   378	                for (size_t j = 0; j < src[k][i].size(); ++j) {
   379	                    dest[k][i][j].resize(src[k][i][j].size());
   380	                    for (size_t l = 0; l < src[k][i][j].size(); ++l) {
   381	                        dest[k][i][j][l] = src[k][i][j][l].ConvertToInt<uint64_t>();  // m_value;
   382	                    }
   383	                }
   384	            }
   385	        }
   386	    }
   387	
   388	    if (cc->GetScheme()->m_FHE) {
   389	        if (boot_conf == FIDESlib::ENCAPS) {
   390	            // lbcrypto::FHECKKSRNS::g_coefficientsSparseEncapsulated
   391	            result.coefficientsCheby = {
   392	                0.24554573401685137,    -0.047919064883347899,   0.28388702040840819,      -0.029944538735513584,
   393	                0.35576522619036460,    0.015106561885073030,    0.29532946674499999,      0.071203602333739374,
   394	                -0.10347347339668074,   0.044997590512555294,    -0.42750712431925747,     -0.090342129729094875,
   395	                0.36762876269324946,    0.049318066039335348,    -0.14535986272411980,     -0.015106938483063579,
   396	                0.035951935499240355,   0.0031036582188686437,   -0.0062644606607068463,   -0.00046609430477154916,
   397	                0.00082128798852385086, 0.000053910533892372678, -0.000084551549768927401, -4.9773801787288514e-6,
